Professor MORRISON, Entrusted with Roosevelt's Mission, Arrives in England and Turkey 33

Will replace HULL as the Chief Representative

Attending the World Economic Conference

US Undersecretary of State MORRISON boarded the "Manhattan" postal ship and arrived here today, and will continue on the original ship to Plymouth, where he is expected to arrive at around 5 p.m. (National Telegram, 27th)

London Professor MORRISON, a close advisor to President Roosevelt, was originally scheduled to arrive in Plymouth at 6 p.m. tonight. According to news from the US Embassy, Morrison will disembark in Queenstown, Ireland, and then take a seaplane to London. Professor Morrison came to London on behalf of President Roosevelt on a mission related to the World Economic Conference and is expected to replace Secretary of State HULL as the US Chief Representative at the conference. HULL will return to Washington earlier (Reuters, 27th).

US Inflation Threatens International Exchange Market 34

The Netherlands and Switzerland May be Forced to Abandon the Gold Standard

British Pound Policy Controls European Financial Situation

London Today, the Dutch and Swiss currencies plummeted, causing fears that the Netherlands and Switzerland would be forced to abandon the gold standard, and the International Economic Conference focused on this crisis. The European gold standard countries are worried about being forced to abandon the gold standard. This afternoon, they urgently requested British Prime Minister MacDonald to clearly inform them of Britain's future gold pound policy. The key members of the central banks of France, Belgium, Switzerland, Netherlands and Germany held a secret meeting this morning and are deeply worried that Britain will also imitate the US President's inflation policy, devaluing the pound, which would increase the tension of gold in Europe and make it impossible to maintain the gold standard. Therefore, they asked Britain to explain its attitude. In addition, it was decided to take steps to maintain the gold standard and discuss self-defense plans. This afternoon, it was also heard that British Prime Minister MacDonald, in view of the Netherlands and Switzerland being forced to abandon the gold standard, will use his qualifications as the chairman of the Economic Conference to ask them to maintain the gold standard. According to the opening prices this morning, the Dutch currency was 8.565 and the Swiss franc was 17.66. The closing prices yesterday were 8.58 and 17.665. The opening prices at 2 pm today fell again to 8.52 and 17.64 (National Telegram, 27th).

Amsterdam The decision of the Dutch bank to only exchange cash in the morning has caused fears of inflation among the people here. This afternoon, the public did not know the implementation of the new chapter and was worried that the Netherlands would stop paying cash, but the bank has now stated that it will exchange cash as usual tomorrow. After the bank stopped exchanging cash in the afternoon, the prices of British, American, and French currencies have all risen (Reuters, 26th).

London This morning, the economic conference was very concerned about the threat of US inflation and the recent currency changes. The fall of the Dutch currency yesterday was quite pessimistic in some respects. The situation of the economic conference depends heavily on the attitude of the UK. If the UK can guarantee to maintain the price of gold pounds, the general worries can be immediately eliminated. Unfortunately, the UK does not seem to be willing to abandon its traditional policy of observing the situation. In addition, the general public hopes that the arrival of US representative Morrison in the UK can bring some comfort regarding the US monetary policy, but public opinion is very skeptical about this (Havas, 27th).

US Prices Continue to Rise and Accelerate, Starting the Wheels of Industrial and Commercial Recovery 35

Washington Today, official news, although the US President is unwilling to continue inflating the currency to maintain prices, if the progress of commercial recovery encounters obstacles, he will use his power to inflate the currency to eliminate the obstacles. However, since the US government implemented the first step of the inflation program, the price increase and increased employment achieved have been stimulated by other aspects and have been able to remain strong so far. After this national heatwave, grain prices have risen accordingly, and the implementation of the federal unemployment relief program has caused the need for machinery, clothing, and raw materials. Private inventories have been sold out. According to the Ministry of Commerce, there has been real progress in the domestic economic situation. Therefore, the President now believes that the inflation program has started the wheels of industrial and commercial recovery. If it encounters unexpected obstacles, it will have to inflate the currency again to maintain it. However, officials believe that there should be no need to inflate the currency again. Because the Midwest has experienced a heatwave and drought not seen in 30 years, livestock and wheat harvests have been greatly affected. It is expected that grain prices will be high in the future. If the southern cotton fields are destroyed by a quarter as planned by the President, the prices of ordinary goods that are transferred by the prices of wheat and cotton will be able to remain firm (National Telegram, 26th).

Various Subcommittees Continue Routine Work 36

London The various subcommittees of the World Economic Conference continued to reconcile differing opinions on important issues today. The Trade Committee discussed bilateral and multilateral commercial agreements. Representatives mostly favored bilateral agreements. The German representative stated that Germany advocated multilateral commercial agreements because it needed to balance its import and export trade and because of its agricultural needs. Representatives from Hungary, Poland, and other agricultural countries had the same proposal. The Monetary Committee discussed the minimum limit for issuing banknotes and gold reserves and decided that the law regulating this ratio should be flexible. The Silver Committee also exchanged the draft principles developed last week regarding regulating the balance between supply and demand in the silver market. The committee decided to send the report back to the drafting committee (National Telegram, 26th).

Monetary Treatment Subcommittee

British and American Opinions Differ on the Issue of International Commercial Debt 37

Chamberlain Explains that the Position of Creditor Countries Should Restore Credit The US Representative Proposes Raising Prices and Reorganizing Debt Together

London When the First Monetary Subcommittee of the World Economic Conference discussed ways to raise prices today, a new problem arose due to differences of opinion between Chamberlain and Coughton, which will be studied by the conference. The question is whether world prices can be fully increased before reducing international commercial debts, or whether debts must be reorganized first before joint efforts can be made to raise prices. Chamberlain believed that world prices were already on an upward path and that the need for debt reduction may be reduced in the future after prices have generally risen. Coughton argued that prices can never be fully increased to balance existing international debts. Therefore, prices must be increased and debts must be reduced. Both must be carried out at the same time to succeed. Coughton then explained the US government's plan to raise prices, saying that he knew that Europeans believed that the US would inflate the currency to raise prices, but this path is not the main road. The US government believes that the fundamental goal is to increase production and consumption, so that prices can rise and purchasing power can also increase. He then explained that two-thirds of the raw materials used in the US are imported duty-free, and the federal unemployment relief program can increase the demand for raw materials. Coughton advocated that creditors organize an international agency to study and propose methods to reduce debts. Chamberlain believed that this matter should be negotiated directly between creditors and debtors (according to the US attitude toward war debts, it is the same as Chamberlain's proposal). Chamberlain also wanted an international agency, but insisted that it should be purely advisory and should not be given the power to conclude agreements, saying that Britain could not allow international groups to supervise its debts and its general relations. Chamberlain then discussed the relationship between national debts and general debts, advising countries to be more cautious in issuing public bonds in the future and to pay attention to the appropriate protection of subscribers. Both agreed that it would be very difficult to find a satisfactory solution to commercial debts. Coughton also stated that the US or other creditor countries' willingness to reduce debt should not be regarded as an invitation for debtors to rely on debt. Debt must be reduced only if the debtor is unable to repay it. According to the original hope of the representatives today that Chamberlain would express Britain's attitude towards the US proposal to encourage countries to adopt domestic programs to reduce unemployment and raise prices, but the two sides only debated the issue of commercial debt, Chamberlain stated that the British representatives still need to study the US proposal, which disappointed other representatives (National Telegram, 26th).

London The monetary sub-committee of the Economic Conference met to discuss the debt issue, British Chancellor Chamberlain briefly explained the position of the creditor countries to answer the opinions raised by the debtor countries, briefly saying "In recent years, the history of foreign loans has not made the lending countries have credit, and the disappearance of credit has made the capital problem upside down" Chamberlain then expressed sympathy to the debtor countries, especially to the countries that export raw materials and agricultural products. Chamberlain believed that raising prices is the best and permanent way to relieve the debt problem. As for the application method, he advocated that the debtor and creditor countries sign bilateral agreements, but for it to succeed, it is more appropriate for the representatives of the creditor countries to organize a fair consulting agency so that all parties can be satisfied, but this agency has no arbitral nature. Chamberlain believes that bringing all creditors together regardless of national boundaries will inevitably lead to useless disputes, which is contrary to the opinion of the Hungarian representative Onai. Chamberlain finally said that the countries had previously provided assistance to the debtor countries and can still provide new assistance in the future. He hoped that the debtor countries will do their best to live up to the credit of the countries (Havas, 26th).

France and Italy Support British Proposals 38

London Today, Italian and French representatives fully supported the policy of British Chancellor Chamberlain yesterday, which stated that temporary reorganization should be given to international commercial debts when necessary and did not approve of the permanent reduction proposal held by US representative Coughton. French Finance Minister Ponet stated that France always supports the policy of reorganizing debts to stabilize currencies, believing that there is no need to reduce international commercial debts, only generous conditions need to be adopted. Under this kind of action, it is expected that the wheels of commerce will be started and trust will be restored. However, when fulfilling debts, debtors should be given sufficient opportunities to restore their normal economic conditions. Creditors must assist debtors and give them the greatest convenience in export trade. Coughton also strongly requested to stabilize currencies. He believed that it is rare to have permanent success unless all countries stabilize currencies together. The president of the Swiss National Bank, SARASIN, also fully supported Chamberlain's proposal. After Sarasit's speech, the subcommittee made a brief general debate and elected a drafting committee to draft a proposal, and adjourned at 11:45 am (National Telegram, 27th).

Monetary Treatment Subcommittee 39

Expert Committee Passes Resolution

Advocating Reduction of Legal Gold Reserves

London This morning, the World Economic Conference had a very interesting development. The expert committee of the Monetary Committee has passed a resolution, advocating that gold coins and gold coupons should not be circulated domestically, and advocating that the consistent gold reserve of the central bank should not exceed 25%. However, this kind of flexibility should not be used as an excuse to excessively expand the quantity of banknotes and credit. This proposal will be submitted to the Second Subcommittee (Reuters, 27th).

Monetary Silver Subcommittee 40

Chairman Resolves Indian Representative's Opinions

London The Silver Subcommittee was originally scheduled to continue its meeting this morning, but it has been postponed until the afternoon so that Chairman Pitman can first have a private meeting with Indian representative Hecht, because after a brief talk between Pitman and Hecht yesterday afternoon, it was discovered that Hecht's speech, which he plans to give at the meeting this morning, has opinions that are very different from Pitman's and are easy to cause a split in the committee (National Telegram, 27th).

Economic and Trade Subcommittee 41

Listening to US Explanation of Tariff Policy

London Economic Committee of the Economic Conference Trade Policy Subcommittee listened to a statement on US tariff policy. Regarding the most-favored-nation clause, no one registered to speak. The meeting was adjourned and will be held again tomorrow (Havas, 24th).

Sugar Producing Countries Representatives 42

Discuss Limiting Sugar Production

London The representatives of the main countries that signed the sugar production and sales agreement in Brussels previously met here today to discuss the Cuban representative's proposal to the Economic Conference to limit sugar production. At the beginning of the discussion, the Australian representative expressed opposition, saying that since the overproduction of sugar has not been proven, Australia cannot approve of limiting the production of sugar. French representative Sarrot said that a committee must be organized to draft a draft in clearer language for detailed discussion. Subsequently, the Cuban representative proposed a proposal to stabilize sugar prices (National Telegram, 26th).

Moscow Newspaper Discusses Anti-Russian Formation in London 43

Close Collusion Between Britain, Germany, and Japan

Moscow Soviet news circles have already understood the anti-Soviet actions expressed in the recent developments of the London World Economic Conference. This kind of action is reflected in the proposal of the Anglo-German commercial agreement proposed by Germany and in the speeches made by German representative Bose and British and Japanese representatives in the branch committees regarding the issue of most-favored-nation treatment. The Red Army newspaper "Krasnaya Svanstad" stated that the plan proposed by Germany to open up the Soviet market in the middle and Bose's anti-Soviet speech gave a clever supplement to the Hugenberg memorandum, and made the theory of interventionism in the memorandum more developed and specific. The Soviet government gazette "Izvestia" declared that the Soviet Union will find a way to express that the Soviet market should be handled by the Soviet Union itself, and there is no need to trouble other countries from afar. It also pointed out that in the Geneva Conference eleven years ago, the attempt to set an agreement for handling the Soviet market was first revealed, but it still encountered a tragic failure at that time. The Communist Party newspaper Pravda also said that Bose's speech is enough to prove the anti-Soviet nature of the Hugenberg memorandum. The newspaper declared, "German fascism is promoting its anti-Soviet plan in London because London can provide the most suitable atmosphere for the development and growth of this plan. This point is also proven by the speeches of British and Japanese representatives." The newspaper continued, "This kind of combination of Britain, Germany, and Japan is by no means accidental, destroying and showing its essential trend, and expressing the leading role of British imperialism, which is trying to incite Japan against the Soviet Union." Pravda concluded, "German fascism is engaged in adventurous actions again and again. Only those who are dizzy can think of establishing a sphere of influence in the Soviet Union, but they can try it." (TASS, 26th)

Britain's East African Territories Reject Japanese Goods 44

British Mandated Territories to Follow Suit

Japanese Government to Appoint Representative for Negotiations with India

Mombasa, British Territory of Kenya, 26th: It has been decided to impose new high tariffs on imported cotton products and other goods. (26th, Nippon Telegraph & Telephone Corporation dispatch)

Tokyo dispatch: The British colony of Kenya in British East Africa is planning to increase tariffs. The British protectorate of Uganda and the British mandated territory of Tanganyika, which have formed a customs union, will also implement tariff increases. This violates the principle of equal opportunity for development in Africa, including the Congo Treaty area. The Japanese government may lodge a protest on this basis. Last year, Japan's trade with East Africa amounted to 15 million in exports and 3.3 million in imports. (27th, Domei News Agency dispatch)

Tokyo: Kenya, a British territory, is raising tariffs. After the European War, Japan participated in the Congo Treaty based on the principle of equal opportunity to develop Africa. Therefore, it has the right to protest the tariff increase. The Japanese government is likely to lodge a serious protest with Britain. (27th, Nippon Telegraph & Telephone Corporation dispatch)

Tokyo: Today's regular cabinet meeting officially decided on the Japanese representatives to attend the Simla Conference and announced the following appointments: Minister Plenipotentiary Setsuzo Sawada and Shin Terao, Director of the Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry, will serve as Japanese representatives to the Simla Conference. Negotiations are underway with the Chairman of the Textile Federation, Bojiro Abe, as the private sector representative. (27th, Domei News Agency dispatch)

Tokyo: The Japanese government's instructions to be taken to the Simla Conference were reported today at the regular cabinet meeting by Foreign Minister Uchida and Commerce Minister Nakajima, and approval has been obtained. Foreign Minister Uchida will formally hand them over to the two representatives soon. The main points of the instructions are generally as follows: The Japanese government intends to negotiate with the Indian government to conclude a Japan-India treaty or extend the validity of existing treaties based on reciprocity and most-favored-nation treatment as conditions for adjusting current and future relations. If a formal treaty cannot be concluded, a de facto provisional agreement including the following points regarding Japan-India commercial, navigation, and tariff relations will be sought, pledging to conclude a formal treaty in the future. In light of the economic conditions in Japan and India, mutual recognition and restrictions on most-favored-nation treatment will be considered. Mutually beneficial measures will be sought for goods imported and exported by both sides. For example, the Indian government should reduce tariffs on cotton products and consider the allocation of imports. The Japanese government guarantees the allocation of Indian cotton imports and considers reducing tariffs on pig iron and other items. The Imperial government will encourage the control of exports by private businesses, and the Indian government should follow suit to show sincerity. If Japan-India trade relations break down, the responsibility lies with India. (27th, Domei News Agency dispatch)

Using the Pretext of Investigating the Murder of Fishermen, Japanese Torpedo Boats Entered Russian Territorial Waters 45

The Soviet Government Lodges a Serious Protest

Accuses Japanese Soldiers of Landing, Violating International Law

Japanese Naval Authorities Take a Strong Stance, Saying They Will Take Self-Defense Actions by Force 46

Moscow: In an exchange of views between Japanese Ambassador Ota and Soviet Deputy Commissar for Foreign Affairs Sokolnikov, it was revealed that the Japanese Ryufu torpedo boat recently disregarded the lack of consent from the Soviet government, entered Soviet waters off Kamchatka, and claimed to be investigating the fact that Soviet coastal guards shot and killed three Japanese fishermen on June 10. It even landed a team of personnel on Soviet territory. On June 21, Ota protested to Sokolnikov regarding the shooting of three fishermen at Kronotsky Cape in the Kamchatka Peninsula, as claimed by Ota, and requested that Sokolnikov allow the secretary of the Japanese consulate in Petropavlovsk to board the Ryufu torpedo boat and go to the scene to verify the shooting. Sokolnikov told Ota that the Soviet government had not yet received a report on this matter. If the facts are as Ota said, the perpetrators will be identified and appropriately punished. However, Sokolnikov resolutely rejected the suggestion that the secretary of the Japanese consulate travel to the scene on a warship. Finally, he and Ota agreed that the secretary could be sent by civilian ship, and at the same time, local Soviet authorities were immediately instructed to go to the scene to conduct an investigation. This shows that a proper way to resolve the dispute has been jointly established by Sokolnikov and Ota regarding the protest raised by Japan regarding this incident. However, the Ryufu torpedo boat, without waiting for the results of the Soviet investigation or the arrival of the secretary of the Japanese consulate, immediately penetrated waters within Soviet territory and landed a team of personnel, arbitrarily surveying the coastline on Soviet territory. Sokolnikov and Ota have already discussed this action. The Soviet protest is as follows: "According to the Soviet government's preliminary investigation, there are no Soviet coastal guards in the deserted Kronotsky Cape area. Therefore, the Soviet government is deeply perplexed by the Japanese government's protest regarding the shooting of three Japanese fishermen by Soviet coastal guards in that area. The Soviet government has not continued to receive reports sufficient to confirm the shooting. However, if a subsequent investigation confirms the facts claimed by Ota and establishes the guilt of Soviet citizens, the criminals will undoubtedly be properly punished. But at present, the Soviet government has not yet verified this matter. At the same time, the Soviet government feels it necessary to seriously protest the actions of the Japanese torpedo boat, which violated strict and indisputable legal norms. This action makes it difficult for the Soviet authorities responsible for investigating the alleged killing of three fishermen (if such an incident did occur). At the same time, the Soviet government cannot help but express its surprise at the denial made by the Director of the Eurasian Department of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Spier van Neck, Counselor of the Soviet Embassy in Tokyo, on June 20 that the torpedo boat had entered Soviet territorial waters. What surprises the Soviet Union even more is the falsehood in the report made by the Director of the Information Bureau of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs to foreign journalists. He said that on June 21, the Japanese Ambassador in Moscow had reported to the People's Commissariat for Foreign Affairs that the Japanese torpedo boat had entered Soviet territorial waters. In fact, regarding this action that has already caused the Soviet government to lodge a serious protest, the Soviet government has not received any report from the Japanese Embassy. The fact is that it was heard from the statement of the Director of the Information Bureau of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs," etc. (26th, TASS dispatch)

Tokyo: The Soviet Union has lodged a counter-protest against the entry of the Japanese destroyer Tachikaze into Russian territorial waters, claiming it violated international law. Japanese naval authorities categorically refuted this, saying that the Tachikaze rushed to the area to search for the perpetrators and collect corpses after receiving an urgent report from the Fumimaru that it was under unlawful fire from the Soviet Union. They also obtained evidence. When a fishing boat is in danger, the patrol ship naturally has the duty to provide protection. Its actions were entirely an exercise of the right to self-defense. If the Soviet Union does not show sincerity and ignores this incident, the Navy will increase the deployment of patrol ships and take active patrol actions to protect Japanese fishing boats by force. (27th, Domei News Agency dispatch)

Xiao Lifen Inspects Construction of Hangzhou-Jiangshan Road 62

Disarmament Decides to Adjourn 81

▲ Paris dispatch, 26th (National news agency): The Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, Henderson, met with French Foreign Minister Pongou today. They reached an agreement regarding the postponement of the Disarmament Conference. Henderson will submit this proposal to the core committee in Geneva and advocate for a postponement until after the League of Nations conference in September or October.

▲ Geneva dispatch, 27th (Havas news agency): Work on the Disarmament Conference has resumed. The Presidium is scheduled to meet at 3 PM this afternoon. There is much debate in the conference lounge. After exchanging opinions, the majority of delegations favor postponing the Disarmament Conference. The Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, Henderson, also expressed the same view. The U.S. delegation appears to be unconcerned about the disarmament issue, believing that the European countries should decide on their own. This attitude indicates that the U.S. position has changed, as not long ago, the U.S. representative to the Disarmament Conference, Davis, actively participated in disarmament efforts. As for Germany, it will continue to oppose postponing the Disarmament Conference. However, this is the second time Germany has opposed the postponement, and even the German delegation does not believe that its opposition will be taken seriously in Geneva. Furthermore, the League of Nations Secretariat issued a statement claiming that it had received approximately seventy telegrams from various parts of Germany, all reporting the issue of unidentified aircraft flying in German airspace. All parties are paying close attention to this statement. The "National Daily" published an article commenting on this matter, stating that the publication of this statement was a formal order from the highest level. The League of Nations Secretariat attaches such importance to the seventy telegrams from Germany, but countless petitions from people everywhere to the League of Nations, recounting the brutal acts of the current German regime, have been ignored. How can there be such inconsistency and contradiction in the world? The League of Nations has not yet issued a statement regarding the atrocities of the current German regime, but now, before the reopening of the Disarmament Conference, it is discussing Germany's demand for rearmament, allowing armies that specialize in massacring defenseless people to achieve their desires. The intentions are beyond our comprehension.

▲ Paris dispatch, 26th (Havas news agency): British Under-Secretary of State for Foreign Affairs, Eden, is traveling to Geneva to attend the Presidium meeting of the Disarmament Conference. In addition, the head of the British Affairs Office of the League of Nations, Ketogen, is also traveling to Geneva with Eden. The two visited Foreign Minister Pongou here this evening, and Pongou granted them an audience.

▲ London dispatch, 27th (Reuters news agency): Baldwin denied in the House of Commons today that the London talks on the Disarmament Conference have been abandoned, stating that these talks have only been temporarily delayed due to the activities of the World Economic Conference. The British government firmly believes that these talks are necessary for the good progress of the Disarmament Conference. As for the rumors that the opening date of the conference will be postponed until the autumn, this remains to be confirmed.

Feng Yuxiang Actively Plans Resistance Against Japan 87

Ji Hongchang's Troops Advance in Five Routes Towards Kangbao

Liu Guitang Defects and Leads Troops to Guyuan

Special dispatch from Beiping: Since the 21st, the atmosphere in the Zhangjiakou area has suddenly changed, with active plans for resistance against Japan. Feng Yuxiang, in the name of the Commander-in-Chief of the Anti-Japanese Allied Army, appointed Li Zhenwu as the Commander-in-Chief of the Northern Route Anti-Japanese Army and Ji Hongchang as the Commander-in-Chief of the Front. Ji carried his entourage to Zhangjiakou early on the 22nd to deploy everything, arrived at noon, and immediately organized the General Headquarters in Zhangbei, took the oath of office, and issued an inaugural telegram. His troops are divided into five routes: the first route is Deng Wen's, the second route is Li Zhongyi's, the third route is Zhou Rongxuan's, the fourth route is Nie Yuling's, and the fifth route is Hu Yunshan's. Deng Wen and other troops are currently concentrating in Zhangbei and will advance towards Kangbao and Baochang in the near future, preparing to recover Duolun. Fang Zhenwu is still in Zhangjiakou, discussing with Feng. Fang's division under Zhang Renjie opened to the vicinity of Zhangjiakou a few days ago and is also preparing to advance towards the Zhangdu Avenue. If necessary, Fang will also go to the front to inspect. The cavalry army under Zhao Chengshou, originally stationed in Zhangbei, has been ordered by the Beiping Military Branch Council to be stationed in Nanhouchang, which is between Kangbao and Shangdu, about three hundred li from Zhangbei. They are currently relocating. Zhao himself is still in Zhangbei and will inspect the cavalry stationed there in Pingdiquan after his troops have completed their departure.

Since the signing of the ceasefire agreement, the Japanese army has been carrying out an invasion plan for Chahar. On the one hand, they are reinforcing troops in Duolun, and on the other hand, they are instigating rebel troops such as Liu Guitang and Cui Xinwu to advance westward and create disturbances, in order to achieve their poisonous plan of using Chinese to control Chinese. After Liu Guitang led his troops to occupy Baochang and Kangbao, they did not advance. At this time, Feng Yuxiang established the Anti-Japanese position in Zhangjiakou, uniting various armies and advocating resistance against Japan. Liu repeatedly sent personnel to express his surrender. Finally, he sent his Deputy Army Commander Shang Wu to Zhangjiakou to meet with Feng and explain everything, saying that Liu was isolated from the main army in Northern Shandong, and in order to preserve his strength and slowly plan to serve the country, he feigned cooperation with the Japanese army. Since entering Chahar, he has been oppressed by the Japanese army and has not been understood by the national army, and he has no way to justify himself. Now, he is willing to lead his troops to listen to commands and unite to resist Japan. Feng said that he was taking on the task of resisting Japan from the standpoint of the people, and if they could share the same ideals, they could turn enemies into friends. The negotiations between the two sides were quite satisfactory. Now, Feng and Liu have agreed that Liu will give up the defense area around Baochang and Kangbao, which will be stationed by Feng's troops, in order to facilitate the recovery of Duolun. Liu's troops will then open to Guyuan to attack Rehexi. On the morning of the 23rd, the troops of Liu Guitang around Kangbao and Baochang moved towards Guyuan. The various armies of Feng's Ji Hongchang and Deng Wen, as well as the reorganized volunteer army, are concentrating in Zhangbei, preparing to be stationed in Kangbao and Baochang, etc., to realize the recovery of the lost land in Eastern Chahar and directly attack Duolun. The Japanese army in Duolun is stationed with a cavalry unit under Motegi, as well as more than 2,000 rebel troops under Cui Xingwu. The military strength is weak. The rebel troops under Cui also have a tendency to surrender and have sent representatives to contact Ji Hongchang. To what extent the situation in Eastern Chahar will develop in the future will be clear during the most knowledgeable period. (Arrived on the 25th)

Yangtze River Water Level Stabilizes 88

Wuhan Still Submerged; Dikes in Various Counties in Danger

General Headquarters Orders Flood Control Personnel to Diligently Attend to Their Duties

Police Department Forbids Digging of Dikes; Violators to Be Executed on the Spot

Provincial Government Requests Economic Council to Issue 200,000 in Flood Control Funds

Hankou Correspondence: For half a month, the water level of the Yangtze River at various ports has been increasing without decreasing. It only gradually stabilized on the 25th. Hankou and Hanyang only each saw a four-inch rise in water level. On the 26th, Hankou maintained a water mark of 47 feet and 2 inches, with no rise or fall compared to the 25th. Chongqing was at 30 feet and 8 inches, Yichang at 32 feet and 4 inches, Changsha at 24 feet and 7 inches, Yuezhou at 49 feet and 1 inch, Shashi at 28 feet, and Jiujiang at 44 feet and 2 inches. The water levels were the same as on the 25th. Downstream, Wuhu and Zhenjiang each rose by 4 inches, which is not surprising as the water is receding. However, the clear weather suddenly turned cloudy and rainy. If it continues for several days, the water source will increase again. Whether the disaster situation will expand in the future is not something that can be predicted at this time. Wuhan and the three towns are still in the vast floodwaters as the water has not receded slightly. The dikes and sluices in the suburbs are still not out of danger and are currently being protected separately by the Flood Control Association, the Construction Department, and the Municipal Government. If the water does not rise any further, there should be no worries. The Wuhan Garrison Headquarters has issued a notice to various garrison agencies and troops to strictly patrol the various dike projects. If any malicious individuals are found stealing and digging into the dikes, they will be executed on the spot. In various counties, in addition to the early collapse of the Jinshui New Dam and the Zhang Daonan Dike in Shishou, the Xinchun, Sanxing, and Yagong dikes have also continued to collapse. In addition, the water level of the main dikes of Jianli Chewan and the Xin Dike Jingjiang is higher than the dikes, and there are many leaks. The Du Long Dike and Great Wall in Huanggang are too heavily impacted and are all in danger. The Mahua Dike and Jingjiang Dike, which are related to the livelihood of seven counties in three provinces, are especially precarious. Representatives from Susong, Huangmei, Jiujiang, Pengze, Guangji, Taihu, and Wangjiang sent telegrams to the governments of Hubei, Jiangxi, and Anhui on the 26th, requesting that Commander-in-Chief Chiang be telegraphed to order the National Economic Council to quickly allocate large sums of money to carry out rescue work. The telegram stated, "To the Chairman of the Hubei Provincial Government, Xia; the Chairman of the Jiangxi Provincial Government, Xiong; and the Chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, Liu Junjian: Since the beginning of summer this year, there has been torrential rain, and the river has been soaring. The water has risen more than a foot in one day and one night. Currently, the Jingjiang and Mahua dikes are submerged by as much as six to seven feet. It is difficult for these unconsolidated sand dikes to withstand the waves of the south wind. If the water rises again, it will inevitably overflow the dikes and rush straight in. Then the refugees in the seven counties of the three provinces will once again be buried in the belly of the fish. The association has personally supervised nearby residents, patrolling day and night, and devising ways to protect them. For this reason, a report is made to urgently request that Commander-in-Chief Chiang be telegraphed to order the National Economic Committee to order the engineering bureaus of Anhui and Jiangxi to bring funds to the dikes and rebuild them as before to save the emergency and focus on the dikes. The surviving people of the three provinces and seven counties are grateful for the vast contributions. Wu Xiaoyun, Chairman of the Susong Jingma Dike Construction Committee; Wu Shangda, representative of the Huangmei Jiang Dike; Zhuo Er, representative of the Jiujiang Jiang Dike; Hong Chunmao, representative of the Pengze Jiang Dike; Wang Qing, representative of the Guangji Jiang Dike; Yu Jiude, representative of the Taihu Jiang Dike; and Yang Ren, representative of the Wangjiang Jiang Dike."

Shen Honglie Attacked by Assassin 89

=The Assassin Was the Gunner on the Zhenhai Warship=

Several Shots Fired at Shen All Missed

Feng Zhichong Fell into the Sea but Was Still Arrested=

Qingdao Correspondence: Yesterday (the 24th) at 4:40 PM, Shen Honglie, the Mayor of Qingdao and Commander of the Bohai Fleet, after participating in the swimming preliminaries at the Qianhai, accompanied by his adjutant Shi Liangzuo, took a car to the Second Pier for inspection. The Zhenhai warship belonging to the Bohai Fleet was moored at the Fourth Pier, and a small steam launch was dispatched to the shore to welcome Shen aboard. While en route, Feng Zhichong (33 years old, from Liaoning), the gunner on the warship, suddenly used a box gun with live ammunition to shoot at Shen in the cabin. Fortunately, Adjutant Shi spotted him and immediately threw Feng into the sea. After falling into the sea, Feng continued to fire three shots at the small steam launch, all of which missed. Feng was then arrested and taken to the Naval Headquarters for strict interrogation. No reliable confession has yet been obtained. It is not yet known whether there is a political background to this matter. Shen still went to the Zhenhai warship to give a speech, which ended at 6:00 PM. He remained unusually calm and returned to his residence safely. After this incident, a special curfew was temporarily imposed in the Dagang area, and all idlers entering and leaving the pier were subjected to thorough searches. There was a disturbance for half the night, but no further clues were obtained. However, according to news from the municipal government, the assassin had old grudges with Adjutant Shi and intended to attack Shi this time to avenge his past grievances, but mistakenly targeted Shen. Wuxi 90

Shipping Industry Protests Defense Levy

The Wuxi County Government decided at a county government meeting to levy a defense fee of five cents per yuan on all passenger ships starting on July 1st and instructed the county chamber of commerce to notify each ship separately. A notice has also been issued. After receiving the notice, the shipping companies believed that the shipping industry depends entirely on freight transportation. In recent years, the market has been declining and has been greatly affected. In addition, the round-trip discounts of trains have led to a rush to road transportation by merchants. The rural economy is declining, and there are fewer passengers on rural routes. If another five cents per yuan is levied on tickets, it will inevitably become impossible to survive. They are especially afraid that this will set a precedent. They immediately convened an emergency meeting. Everyone agreed that this matter concerns the lifeline of the shipping industry and that, according to Article 6 of the Temporary Regulations on Revising and Supervising Local Finance promulgated by the Legislative Yuan, regulations that hinder traffic taxes and levies should not be implemented, and that the levy should be stopped. Yesterday, they sent separate telegrams to the Executive Yuan in Nanjing, as well as the Ministry of Communications, the Jiangsu Provincial Government, and the Construction Department, requesting a swift stop to maintain the industry.

Later, the trip was canceled as the Chahar situation eased. This time, key figures in the central government telegraphed Kong again, reiterating the previous request. Kong was originally scheduled to take a plane from Hongqiao Airport to Beiping at 8:30 AM yesterday morning, arriving in the afternoon. After meeting with He Yingqin and Huang Fu, he would transfer to Shanxi to meet with Yan and urge Yan to come forward to mediate the Chahar situation so that the situation would not escalate and peace would be realized as soon as possible. However, due to the overcast weather yesterday morning, it was not suitable for flying, and the trip was temporarily postponed. This morning, it is hoped that the flight will take off. According to Kong, he will go north as soon as the weather clears, and the trip can be made tomorrow or the day after tomorrow.

Xi Dejiong Telegrams That the Dangerous Situation in Wuhan Has Passed 98

Downstream is Critical; Sends Personnel with Materials to the Rescue

Main Dikes Are Solid and Intact; No Damage

This year's early summer flood has caused the water level of the Jianghan to rise daily, setting a new record for the highest water level in the same month in sixty years. Hubei Province, with its rivers and lakes, is most concerned about flooding and relies entirely on dikes for protection. Xi Dejiong, the Chief of the Engineering Department of the National Economic Council, flew to Wuhan the previous week to inspect dike construction and supervise the Jianghan Engineering Bureau in handling flood control matters, establishing an office within the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to personally guide everything. Yesterday, Xi telegraphed the National Economic Council in Shanghai, reporting that the main dikes he built were undamaged when the water was not rising and that the downstream was critical. The original telegram is recorded as follows (title omitted): "Amid the rising waters, Wuhan and its surrounding areas frequently report dangerous situations. However, the main dikes are as solid and intact as before, with no areas submerged. Flood control work is nearing completion, and the water situation is gradually easing. The flood control dikes and the Zhanggong Dike are still eight feet to more than ten feet above the water surface. The Longwang Temple above the Customs is two feet to five feet above. Only the Jiang'an of the Special Zone and the concession is almost at the same level. The beaches of Baisha Island above Wuchang and Parrot Island in Hanyang (all outside the dikes) have been flooded, but the dikes are also intact. The water level here has been flat since yesterday. The dangerous situation upstream has passed. The areas around Fankou and Tuanfeng downstream are still in critical condition. Reliable personnel have been dispatched with materials to assist in the rescue." (Omitted below) In addition, the Economic Committee did not receive water level reports from Hankou and Jiujiang yesterday. Only Wuhu telegraphed that the water level at 7:00 AM was 27.4 feet, continuing to rise by more than two feet from the previous day.

Tianchu Company Aircraft Shipped to Airport for Assembly 99

Once Assembly is Complete

Naming Ceremony to Be Scheduled

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the Junkers aircraft ordered from Germany by Tianchu MSG Factory arrived in Shanghai on the 20th. Due to import passport procedures, it could not be immediately retrieved. These procedures have now been completed, and the factory has submitted a request to the Aviation Association for acceptance. The Aviation Association has forwarded the request to the Aviation Administration of the Ministry of Military Affairs, which has dispatched personnel to accept the aircraft. The aircraft components have been transported by the Aviation Association to Hongqiao Airport, where personnel from the Junkers factory are responsible for assembly. According to the person in charge of the factory, the factory is willing to be responsible for repaying any amount lacking in addition to the 100,000 dollars.

Effectiveness of Telegraph Trunk Line Improvement 100

Increased Efficiency in Communications with Hubei and Fujian

A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency visited Mr. Hua Shijian, the Business Director of the Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, yesterday morning. He spoke in great detail about the improvement of the Shanghai-Hankou trunk line, the Chongqing branch line, and the measures taken to prevent damage to the trunk line during the heavy floods. Details are as follows:

Route Improvement 101

It is said that the Ministry of Communications has been paying close attention to the work of improving routes recently. Three lines have been completed: 1) The Shanghai-Hankou trunk line. Communication between Shanghai and Hankou is one of the most developed telegraph lines in the country, with daily revenue of over 2,000 yuan. Therefore, the position of this line is also extremely important. The line is a duplex system, capable of sending and receiving 100 words each per minute. However, sometimes due to current leakage, it often cannot send and receive in both directions, but only in one direction, which delays the time considerably. The Ministry of Communications specially dispatched Chief Engineer Zhao Lusheng to Shanghai to send personnel to actively repair it. It has now been completely repaired, and the development of telegraph services will no longer be hindered. 2) The Chongqing branch line. The section from Badong to Wushan, about 100 li long, was destroyed by bandits in Sichuan province three years ago. Due to the lack of bandit suppression, it was impossible to repair it. After the bandits were wiped out in January this year, personnel were immediately sent to repair it. The loss was about 50,000 yuan. A report was received yesterday that the line has been repaired, and communication from Hankou to Chongqing can now be directly achieved. 3) The Shanghai-Fujian line. The line from Shanghai to Fujian is subject to moisture and blockage every year during the rainy season. After the Ministry of Communications sent personnel to repair it, the same problems have not occurred this year after the rainy season began.

Flood Prevention 102

It is also said that during the floods of the previous years, many telegraph lines on the Shanghai-Hankou trunk line were damaged by the floods. Since this month, there have been continuous heavy rains and flash floods. Although it has not yet become a major disaster, the situation is also very dangerous. Therefore, in order to prevent problems before they occur, the Ministry of Communications ordered the original four engineers stationed along the line from Shanghai to Zhenjiang, from Zhenjiang to Wuhu, from Wuhu to Jiujiang, and from Jiujiang to Xingguo Wuxue to the terminal point of Hankou, to lead the staff to inspect the line in rotation every five days. As of today, no damage has occurred. However, most of the telegraph poles are planted along the riverbank. If the water level continues to rise and the embankment is not strong and is washed away by the water, the telegraph poles planted on the embankment will also be difficult to avoid falling.

North China Telegraph 103

Since the signing of the ceasefire agreement, the Ministry of Communications has long been preparing to restore the North China telegraph after the withdrawal of the Japanese troops. However, the Japanese and puppet troops are still lingering and have not withdrawn, so there is no way to start. Therefore, to this day, the North China telegraph can only reach as far east as Lutai and as far northwest as Miyun. The coastal lines from Kaiping Xugezhuang and other places have still not been restored. Therefore, this can only be started depending on the withdrawal situation of the Japanese troops.

New Beijing Steamer Stops Sailing in Ningbo Last Night 104

Responding to Taikoo Dockyard Strike

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the strike of the Nan Hua and other steamers of Taikoo Dockyard in Guangdong has lasted for two weeks and there is still no proper solution. The Ningbo seamen also sent a telegram yesterday to respond. The New Beijing Steamer also went on strike in Ningbo last night. The situation is recorded as follows:

Ningbo Responds After the strike broke out in Guangdong, the Guangdong Seamen's Association sent telegrams to seamen in various places, urging them to assist in the negotiations. Yesterday, the Ningbo Seamen's Association sent a telegram to the Wusong Merchant Steamer Tragedy Relief Association, saying: Ningbo agrees to respond, please send personnel to Ningbo to assist as soon as possible. Yang Yuting of the Ningbo Seamen's Association respectfully requests.

Sending Personnel to Ningbo After receiving the report, the Wusong Steamer Tragedy Relief Association immediately selected Zheng Yuqing, the representative of the Changxing Steamer, and Gao Yongliu, a worker from the Wusong Steamer Disaster, to take the Ningshao Steamer Company's ship to Ningbo at 3:00 PM to report on the progress of the negotiations in Guangdong and assist in the proceedings.

Strike Occurs After the Ningbo Seamen's Association sent a telegram to respond, at 5:00 PM last night, the New Beijing Steamer in Ningbo went on strike just as it was about to set sail. The shipowner urgently telegraphed the company for instructions. Passengers on board refunded their tickets. The company plans to entrust the cargo to China Merchants, Sanbei, Ningshao and other ships for transportation. The ship moved to the outer anchorage, and the situation was very tense.

Chamber of Commerce Fourth General Assembly Resolves to Request the Abolition of Fishery Construction Fees 105

Telegram to the Executive Yuan

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce, based on the resolution of the Fourth General Assembly, requested the abolition of fishery construction fees. The original text is as follows: A submission regarding the matter of requesting. According to the proposal of the Shanghai Fresh Fish Trade Association, the method of collecting fishery construction fees is complicated and harsh. Please submit to the central government to order its abolition. Party and Government Intervene in Public Concession Tram Strike 106

Workers Petitioned the Municipal Party Headquarters Yesterday

According to the Da Gong News Agency, the British-owned Shanghai Tram Company dismissed more than 20 ticket sellers without reason, causing a reaction from all workers and brewing a strike. After discussions between the two parties, it was believed that ticket sellers often steal money, causing great losses to the company, and the bad habit should be fundamentally eliminated. Later, party and government representatives pointed out that workers' wages were meager and their livelihoods were difficult to maintain, so there was theft. Wages should be generally increased, and rules for eliminating theft should be formulated for rectification. The class expressed their approval and agreed to consider and reply. More than 20 dismissed workers, due to livelihood concerns, specially sent ticket sellers No. 261, No. 383, No. 228, No. 176, No. 235, and more than ten others, led by the Water and Electricity Workers' Union of the Third District, to the Municipal Party Headquarters to petition. Zhou Lianze, the Chief Secretary of the People's Movement Section, received them and said that the company had expressed its willingness to accept mediation, and this case should be resolved soon. Please wait patiently for the solution. The workers were satisfied and returned.

North Sichuan Road House Tax Case, Hongkou Organizations Telegram 108

Separately Submitted to the Executive and Supervisory Yuans

Handle According to Law and Uphold Justice

Refute the Finance Bureau Director's Remarks

The Joint Meeting of Representatives of Hongkou Organizations, regarding the North Sichuan Road house tax case, based on the resolution, telegraphed the Executive Yuan and the Supervisory Yuan yesterday, reporting that the municipal authorities' collection of house tax was inappropriate, resulting in a market strike, and requesting that justice be upheld. At the same time, it refuted the remarks made by Cai Zengji, the Director of the Municipal Finance Bureau. The details are recorded on the left.

Telegram to the Executive and Supervisory Yuans 109

A submission regarding the administrative chief ordering subordinates to illegally arrest merchants and people, imprisoning innocent people, and fasting for two days. We appeal for handling according to the law. It is found that the area of North Sichuan Road and Des Voeux Road in this city is not a concession. The issue of the cross-border road has been unresolved for a long time, causing the merchants and people there to be in constant fear for the security of their safety. External insults are not taken care of by anyone. Even a slight carelessness will lead to violence. Considering the past facts, no one does not feel pain. However, the patriotism of the merchants and people there has not been released because of this. For example, during the Qi-Lu war in the thirteenth year of the Republic of China, the Public Works Department built walls to block the alleys of North Sichuan Road, and the Public Works Department compiled house numbers. After the Shanghai war, the shops and residents raised more than 900 yuan to help the Second Precinct of the Fifth District move to the nearby concession. This is also the intention of the merchants and people to ask the government to recover the road rights as soon as possible. How should the municipal government plan to fundamentally solve the problem and seek the safety and welfare of the merchants and people? Now, the municipal government is not doing its duty, and suddenly levies taxes. The significance of the relative rights and obligations is not without question. First, the citizens there are mixed with Chinese and foreigners. Regardless of nationality, the rights enjoyed by the municipal administration are the same. The tax obligation is naturally not an exception because of nationality. However, the municipal government only announces for Chinese citizens and not others, and the significance of the relative rights and obligations is not without question. Second, since the land has become a deformed strange phenomenon, whether the tax can be avoided from being duplicated is also a question that the merchants and people should ask. Third, in summary, it is necessary for the merchants and people there to request the municipal government to postpone the tax collection, and there is absolutely no psychology of resisting the tax. The municipal government should respond to this request. However, before the municipal government has officially responded, the Municipal Public Security Bureau has ordered Chen Jiwu, the director of the Second Precinct of the Fifth District, to forcibly collect donations, illegally arrest, and imprison four merchants and people for more than 24 hours, and has not sent them to court. They even cut off their food and drink for two days and nights. Such illegal abuse of power and inhumane behavior can be seen again under the leadership of our National Government. Is it not strange? To be laughed at by foreign countries, to insult the legacy of the late Prime Minister, and to violate the admonitions of Director Wang, there is nothing more than this. The associations and others are closely related and find it difficult to remain silent. It is appropriate to jointly submit a submission, hoping that "Your Yuan will strictly deal with the illegal, and immediately give the Municipal Public Security Bureau Director a corresponding punishment, and dismiss the Fifth District, Second Precinct Director from office for investigation, in order to warn others. This is a public feeling. This is submitted to the Executive Yuan (Your Yuan) to impeach according to the law, in order to warn others. This is a public feeling. This is submitted to the Supervisory Yuan."

Refute Cai's Remarks 110

In the recent municipal meeting, in order to solve the tax collection problem of the cross-border road construction in the area of North Sichuan Road and Des Voeux Road, the remarks made by Cai Zengji, the Director of the Municipal Finance Bureau, stated that the citizens should have no objection to the relative rights and obligations. According to general common sense, it is in line with national administration and laws. However, the citizens there have a considerable reason for requesting a postponement of the tax collection. Director Cai failed to consider in detail before speaking, and our association expresses deep regret. Regarding the reasons why the citizens there requested a postponement of the tax collection, there are three: 1) The issue of the cross-border road construction has been unresolved for a long time, causing our Chinese merchants and people to be insulted by foreigners from time to time, and they have no way to appeal. Past facts can prove this. 2) The residents there are mixed with Chinese and foreigners. Since the rights to enjoy the municipal administration are the same, the tax obligation is naturally not an exception because of nationality. The municipal government's tax collection announcement only mentions Chinese citizens and not others, which seems unfair. 3) The cross-border disputes have been unresolved for a long time, and the power and responsibility are not unified. Before the citizens have obtained a strong guarantee from the municipal government, they will bear the burden of repeated taxation every day. Director Cai's so-called public security and public use rights, citing the first and second reasons, seems to not recognize this, etc.

Submit to the General Association for Record 111

The Citizens' Federation of the First Special District, Twenty-fifth District Branch, and the Shanghai North Five Districts Chamber of Commerce and other groups, in addition to telegraphing the Executive Yuan and the Supervisory Yuan to uphold justice, and refuting Cai's remarks, specially submitted a submission to the Citizens' General Federation for record yesterday. The original text is as follows: A submission regarding the illegal arrest and imprisonment of shops in the Twenty-fifth District Branch due to requests for postponement of tax collection. The Twenty-fifth District Branch convened a Hongkou District joint meeting on the 28th of this month. Those attending included branches from various districts, who unanimously resolved to do their best to assist, and submitted submissions to the Executive and Supervisory Yuans, and letters to the Municipal Council (omitted). It is appropriate to submit this to your association for record, and request a unanimous claim for justice and jointly discuss the aftermath, which is a public feeling.

Annual Meeting of the Institute of International Affairs 116

Liu Zhan'en to Go to the United States for Publicity

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Asks for Increased Import Tax on Rubber Products 121

Maintaining Sales of Domestic Products Depends on Tax Protection

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance to increase the import tax on rubber products to maintain domestic production. The petition states: This petition is for the matter of a request. It was found that the Chamber convened the fourth session of the members' representatives congress on the 25th of this month. The Shanghai Rubber Products Industry Association submitted a proposal to increase the import tax rate on rubber tires and shoes, stating: (1) Tires are a powerful tool to assist transportation. In the past, when our country's factories could not manufacture them, they all relied on imports from foreign merchants, and money flowed out incalculably. Since Chinese people set up factories to manufacture them themselves, although it has only been a little over a year, the progress of the products is beyond expectation. However, in view of the continuous import of foreign tires, rushing ahead and dumping them at low prices, domestic tires have suffered a major blow. If this continues, the future of domestic products is unimaginable. The fundamental policy of rescuing people's livelihoods is due to the fact that our country has not levied anti-dumping duties on foreign tires, nor has it increased import taxes. (2) Shoes, such as galoshes, sunny and rainy shoes, running shoes, and sneakers, are all daily necessities for people. However, the situation is the same as the plight of the above-mentioned tires. The only slight difference is that the import tax on shoes has been slightly increased this time. However, foreign shoes are indeed considered superior. In order to promote domestic products and guide the nascent industry of Chinese people, the import tax on shoes seems insufficient to achieve protective effects. There is indeed a possibility of foreign goods being dumped at low prices. However, no less than tens of thousands of people depend on rubber shoe factories for a living. If the import tax is not stable for one day, then tens of thousands of workers will be uneasy for one day, which is related to social and people's livelihood order, which is not a trivial matter. At the same time, the Rubber Hardware and Vehicle Materials Industry Association also submitted a proposal, stating that since the September 18th Incident, companies such as Xie Kang Rubber Shop have been manufacturing inner and outer tires for rickshaws and bicycles for one year, which are quite popular with Chinese people. However, due to foreign goods being dumped at low prices, the sales of domestic tires have been hindered. Please forward a request to levy the highest tax rate on imported foreign goods, etc. It was found that rubber products factories in this city have been established one after another in recent years, and it was a time of great prosperity. First, due to foreign dumping, most of these factories have closed down due to sluggish sales. Those with larger scale are also struggling to maintain. All of this has been repeatedly described in newspapers. The requests of the two associations to increase the import tax on foreign tires and to increase the tax on shoes more than the current tariff are for the sake of maintaining the nascent industry. After being submitted to the general meeting for a vote, it was decided to pass the proposal and submit it to the Ministry for review and implementation, which is a public convenience. Respectfully submitted to the Ministry of Finance for review and approval for implementation, which is a public convenience.

Large Quantities of Chinese Silver Ingots Shipped to the United States 125

=Over Eleven Million Shipped in Sixty Days, Four Million More Exported Yesterday and the Day Before, Foreign Merchants Competing to Buy from the Yangtze River and North China=

Recently, the United States has needed silver and has been buying from our country for several months in large quantities. Foreign merchant banks in Shanghai have reported for export no less than twenty batches, and silver ingots are the main export, followed by broken silver and silver bars. Silver dollars account for only a small amount. Yesterday and the day before, a huge amount of silver was shipped to the United States. The details are as follows:

Silver Ingots Already Loaded 126

The shipment of Chinese silver to the United States started on March 18 this year. In the past, only American silver bars were imported and exchanged for gold coins for export. However, the situation changed in mid-March this year. The United States lacked silver and started buying from our country. From March 18 to May 26, this period of over two months, a total of twenty batches of silver ingots were loaded from Shanghai to the United States, with varying amounts. The total estimated value is 11,385,587.87 yuan in national currency. These silver ingots were mostly collected from the interior, loaded in boxes of 3,000 to 4,500 yuan each, and unloaded in New York.

Shipping Vessels 127

The above silver ingots were shipped to the United States by various British and American banks in this port. The Dollar Steamship Line ships carried the most, accounting for about two-thirds. The rest were carried by Changxing, Tianxiang, Osaka, and the Meichuanshi Max Wheel. The freight alone costs about 100 yuan for each box of silver ingots from Shanghai to the United States. The total amount shipped out in June has not yet been calculated and announced.

Exports of the Day Before Yesterday 128

Yesterday and the day before, another 466 boxes of silver ingots were reported by the American Bank of China and shipped to New York on the Taishan Wheel of the Tianxiang Line. The estimated value is 2,098,894.39 yuan, which was exported from Shanghai on the 24th. The next day, the President Coolidge of the Dollar Steamship Line sailed to the United States. Another 400 boxes of silver ingots and silver bars worth an estimated 2 million yuan were also loaded to New York. There was another batch recently loaded for shipment.

Foreign Merchants' Purchases 129

Recently, foreign merchants in Shanghai have flocked to various ports along the Yangtze River and inland areas of North China to collect old silver ingots from the people, gather them, and ship them to the United States. Because these silver ingots are of high quality and standard purity, shipping them to the United States can yield a profit of 7% or 8% after deducting various expenses. Therefore, many silver ingots have been shipped from Hankou, Yantai, and other places, with each batch arriving at the port with 400,000 to 500,000 taels. Once over one million are collected, they are reported for export.

Hua Concession Authorities' Disease Prevention Publicity Meeting 130

Discussing Disease Prevention Methods

The Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, the Public Concession, the French Concession Health Offices, and the Seaport Quarantine Office, because Shanghai has a dense population, and epidemics often occur every summer, causing countless deaths among citizens. Therefore, every year at the beginning of summer, joint meetings are held to discuss disease prevention methods and epidemic relief, and publicity groups are organized to promote disease prevention campaigns to citizens using various methods. This summer is approaching again, and the weather is gradually getting hotter. A joint meeting was convened a few days ago to carry out disease prevention campaigns separately. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 p.m., a publicity meeting was held at the Seaport Quarantine Management Office, No. 2 Beijing Road. Attendees included Li Ting'an, Director of the Municipal Health Bureau, Huang Zifang, Chief of the Health Section of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, Wu Liande of the Seaport Quarantine Office, and representatives of the health departments of the two concession engineering bureaus. The meeting was chaired by Director Li to discuss publicity methods, such as advertisements, books, announcements, and verbal instructions, to advise citizens not to drink raw and cold beverages, and street debris, etc. The meeting adjourned at 4:00 p.m. It is heard that the meeting will hold an expanded meeting again tomorrow (29th) to discuss cooperation methods.

Six Private Electrical Companies Actively Prevent Electricity Theft 131

=Announcing Seven Measures and Rewarding Reports from All Walks of Life=

Shanghai Huashang Electric Company, Zhabei Hydropower Company, Pudong Electric Company, Yihua Electric Company, and Zhenru Electric Company, and other six private electrical companies, have recently seen a surge in electricity theft cases. The companies have suffered considerable losses. In order to prevent imitation and reward citizens for reporting, the above five electrical companies, on the 20th of this month, each sent representatives to convene a meeting at the Huashang Electric Company to discuss countermeasures. Based on Article 14 of the "Regulations on Handling Electricity Theft by Electrical Operators" promulgated by the Construction Committee, seven measures for inspecting electricity theft and rewarding reporting were drafted and approved by the Shanghai Municipal Public Utilities Bureau for record, and it was decided to implement them starting from the first of next month. The relevant clauses are extracted as follows: (Article 1) All private electrical companies in Shanghai (hereinafter referred to as "electrical companies") shall, in accordance with the provisions of Article 14 of the "Regulations on Handling Electricity Theft by Electrical Operators" promulgated by the Construction Committee, jointly formulate these measures. All rewards related to inspecting electricity theft and reporting electricity theft shall be carried out in accordance with these measures. (Article 2) Anyone outside the electrical company who discovers that any electricity user has committed electricity theft may report the facts to the electrical company. The electrical company shall be responsible for keeping the identity of the person reporting electricity theft strictly confidential. (Article 3) The person reporting electricity theft must report the electricity theft method of the electricity user to the electrical company in writing. If a diagram can be drawn, it should be sent together. The communication address should be indicated on this report letter, and it should be signed and sealed as proof for receiving the reward money in the future. (Article 4) After receiving a report from someone reporting electricity theft, the electrical company will immediately send personnel to inspect. After verification and confirmation, 20% of the recovered electricity fee paid by the electricity thief will be extracted and awarded to the person reporting. If the reward money is less than 10 silver dollars, it will be awarded 10 silver dollars as the minimum. (Article 5) After the electrical company discovers conclusive evidence of electricity theft, 20% of the recovered electricity fee paid by the electricity thief will be extracted and awarded to the person who is present at the scene and responsible for providing evidence. If the electricity theft case is filed with the court, the electrical company will reimburse the witness for the travel expenses each time they appear in court, or the travel expenses that have been approved by the electrical company in advance. (Article 6) After the electrical company discovers conclusive evidence of electricity theft, the electrical company will determine the reward methods for the relevant personnel within the company who are involved in handling the case. (Article 7) These measures have been jointly formulated by the Shanghai Huashang Electric Company, Zhabei Hydropower Company, Pudong Electric Company, Xianghua Electric Company, and Zhenru Electric Company, and have been submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Public Utilities Bureau for record. They will be implemented after the announcement. If there are any omissions, they may be amended at any time and submitted for record.

The Truth about the Excavation of Ancient Tombs Inside Xiaobeimen 133

=The Coffin Decayed and Leaked, the Ancient Corpse Was Not Decomposed, There Was Liquid Inside, Superstitious Women and Children Scrambling to Scrape It, Saying It Can Cure Diseases=

丨The Public Security Bureau Pays Attention to Hygiene and Sends Police to Prohibit It丨

Yesterday, an ancient tomb was excavated at Wanzhu Street inside Xiaobeimen. The female corpse was intact and caused a sensation. Yesterday's newspaper also carried various legends. The reporter went to the site for investigation at Shenshi and confirmed that a female coffin was dug out on the afternoon of the day before yesterday. Because the coffin was old and the bottom fell out, the female corpse leaked out. It was indeed not decomposed, but it turned black after being exposed to the air for a while. It has now been reburied in another coffin. The broken coffin left behind has accumulated a thick, yellow-black liquid. At that time, superstitious people spread rumors that this ointment could cure diseases if taken. Therefore, a group of ignorant women and children scrambled to scrape it. The first branch of the second district of the Public Security Bureau, in view of the fact that this liquid was transformed from a corrupt corpse buried underground in the coffin for a long time, and it must contain toxic substances, fearing that the ignorant people would actually take it, would inevitably get sick without being sick, which would be detrimental to public health, has ordered the patrol leader Zhang to take the police to the site to suppress it and explain it to the audience to avoid being harmed by superstition. As for the black water, goldfish, etc. reported, they are completely inaccurate.

Women's Murder of Women 136

Yang Wu's False Accusation Leads to Disaster

Qiu Wang Dies by the Knife

Wang Longguang, a native of Jiangxi, is 53 years old. He lives upstairs in the hall at No. 94 Yifu Lane, Xinmin Road, Zhabei Baoshan Road. His wife, Qiu Wang, is 40 years old. Since their marriage, the couple's relationship has been quite harmonious. Recently, Wang suddenly became entangled with Wu Yang, a woman from the same hometown living in the pavilion room at No. 94. Their clandestine affair has been going on for quite some time. Wu Yihe, Wu Yang's husband, is an unemployed resident. Although he vaguely heard about his wife's improper behavior, he couldn't find any evidence, so he kept it to himself. However, recently, Wang's wife, Qiu Wang, found out about the affair and secretly observed her husband's actions. She discovered that there was indeed a mutual affection between the two. Qiu Wang became extremely jealous and repeatedly tried to create trouble to vent her anger. However, she couldn't find any excuse to start a fight. A few days ago, the weather was hot, and Wu Yang borrowed a bathing basin from Qiu Wang because she didn't have one at home. Inadvertently, she dropped the basin, breaking it. Qiu Wang used this as an excuse to confront Wu Yang, which immediately led to a quarrel. People nearby intervened and stopped them from fighting. However, Qiu Wang was still angry and dissatisfied. Yesterday, at around 5:50 PM, she went to Wu Yang's place again to demand compensation for the basin. Wu Yang completely ignored her, and the two women went from exchanging insults to fighting. Qiu Wang, unable to contain her anger, ran back to her room, grabbed a small knife, and stabbed Wu Yang in the face. However, in a twist, Wu Yang snatched the knife from Qiu Wang and stabbed her in the abdomen. Qiu Wang was unable to dodge and was stabbed in the abdomen, immediately bleeding profusely. She collapsed to the ground and died. Neighbors heard the commotion and immediately reported it to the Second Precinct of the Fifth District. The precinct dispatched police officers to the scene and learned about what had happened. They arrested Wang Longguang, Wu Yang, and Wu Yihe and took them to the precinct for questioning and further action. Qiu Wang's body was guarded by the local Baojia, awaiting forensic examination by the court this morning.

The Core of the Problem 137

The core issue that makes this merger difficult to succeed lies in the placement of personnel. The Gold Exchange proposes the merger with the Commodities Exchange as a condition. However, it is difficult to accommodate all the personnel from the commodities side, and in fact, it is almost impossible. The Commodities Exchange insists that all its employees must be accommodated. If there aren't enough positions, they suggest forming a second gold market. However, the Gold Exchange is reluctant to accept this proposal, creating a deadlock in negotiations.

Requesting Instructions from the Ministry 138

As negotiations between the two exchanges have reached a stalemate, they have reported the situation to the Ministry of Industry and requested a postponement to allow for further negotiations. Both exchanges understand that national laws and regulations must be followed, but the negotiation issues should also be resolved satisfactorily. However, the Ministry has not yet responded to this request. In the meantime, both exchanges continue to operate as usual, maintaining the status quo.

Increased Postage for Nanyang 142

12.5 Cents Per Item

Effective September 1st

Central News Agency: The Ministry of Transportation has approved the Postal Administration's request to increase postage for Nanyang, effective September 1st. According to Bureau Chief Huang Naishu, the postage for Nanyang mail is 10 cents per item, the same as for other overseas mail. However, to provide preferential treatment to overseas Chinese, there was a reduced rate of half price. As the postage for overseas mail has increased to 25 cents, the postage for Nanyang has not been increased at all. Now, due to the significant postal deficit, it is proposed to increase it to 12.5 cents. Although the increase is double, it only affects Shantou, Xiamen, Guangzhou, and other places, and the increase is only half of the 25 cents. After this proposal was made, many overseas Chinese opposed it. The Postal Administration also took into consideration the hardships of the people and repeatedly pleaded for understanding. Fortunately, understanding was reached, and the increase will be implemented in September. This will increase the Postal Administration's revenue by over 100,000 yuan per year.
