Free Talk

On Scolding 222

— Tao Pei

Scolding, undeniably, is an art.

If the saying "words are the voice of the heart" is true, then scolding can be said to be the shadow of the soul: where there is scolding, there is also the soul.

Just as words have a positive and negative side, scolding has a distinction between what is intended within and what is intended outside.

If you scold "The weather is terrible, it's raining again!" This is scolding intended within, because you really hate the rain, and the scolding does not contain the meaning of "Oh, how beautiful, the rain dripping like women's tears!" as praise.

But scolding intended within is not art; what is artistic is scolding intended outside.

If you like to sleep and don't get up until twelve or one o'clock, but you are afraid of being discovered and criticized, then you can scold "I went to see so-and-so at nine o'clock that day, but they hadn't gotten up yet, truly decadent!" This proves that since you went to a friend's house at nine o'clock, you are an incorruptible early riser. If you scold like this, even if someone comes to see you before you get up, they will think your late rising is either because of a headache or because you were writing until dawn; if you say so yourself, it will be even more appropriate, and the idea that you are a sleepyhead will never enter their mind. If you are someone who wants to sleep but can't in reality, you can also scold like this. Anyway, only you know that the meaning of the scolding is not really to express your noble early rising, and at the same time, expressing it like this is not a bad thing, it just proves that late rising is enviable.

Transferring your own weaknesses to others, or to people who have the same weaknesses as you, and using them as the object of your scolding, you can unload your weaknesses one by one from yourself and become a relaxed person.

Scolding, undeniably, is an art.

The Origin of Pure Talk 223

— Yu Dafu

Anyone who knows a little about history knows that pure talk began in the Wei Dynasty, flourished in the Jin Dynasty, and declined in the Chen and Sui Dynasties. The Wei Emperor Wu, who composed poems with a spear across his saddle, actually killed Kong Wenju and harmed Mi Zhengping; the Wei Emperor Wen, who narrated classics and talked about literature, would also boil beans and burn stalks, brothers pressing each other. The fact that literati had to be forced into pure talk here can give an idea of their state of mind. Descending to the Jin Dynasty, the ferocity and cruelty of the Yi Zhao father and son were naturally even greater than those of the Cao Wei. Waving a duster and talking about metaphysics could both avoid disaster and gain fame. How could students not compete to admire this trend and reap both fame and reality? By the time of the Chen and Sui Dynasties, with the country devastated by war, the world in chaos, the bookish literati had no duster to wave and no metaphysics to narrate. The disappearance of pure talk was also a natural consequence, but the literati suffered. Modern pure talk seems to have changed its appearance. What is published in great detail in major and minor newspapers and magazines is mostly (1) natural disasters, (2) sexual sins, (3) the whereabouts and anecdotes of important people, and (4) the simultaneous mockery and scolding, suspected false or real news and criticisms of contemporary literati. "The weather today, ha ha ha," is indeed the ultimate in pure talk, and "There is joy in the teachings of morality, why be like this?" is even more so a subtle and profound, eloquent and passionate article. In the end, is it pure talk that misleads the country, or the country that misleads pure talk? This is really a bit difficult to say.

June 25th,

The Like of Lao Can 224

— Cao Juren

A few days ago, the "Free Talk" published an article on the art of the clown, which was really the most appropriate article for sending off Mr. Hu Shih.

After Hu Shih's departure, the country is suffering from too many, not too few, roles of the clown type, but after Mr. Feng's ridicule, I don't know how many people suspect he is scratching their wounds.

Yesterday, when I flipped through "The Travels of Lao Can," I couldn't help but clap my hands and exclaim in wonder: among literati, there is actually the idea of creating a typical clown, like Lao Can!

What kind of person is Lao Can? He can write poetry, he understands medicine, he can manage rivers, he is good at predicting, and he also works as a Sherlock Holmes, able to detect suspicious cases and save the lives of three people. He has never held any official position, but his letter can reach the palace, reversing a major unjust case that has already been decided, and even Gang Bi, who is so stubborn, cannot but retreat. He has never been worth a penny, only shaking a handbell, but everyone is willing to give him thousands of dollars. He is "in the rivers and lakes, but his heart is in the court," a hermit of the mountains and forests, but constantly circling in the political vortex. Saying he is idle, he is really busy; saying he is busy, he is very free. The ideal character under Liu Tieyun's pen is also a typical character admired by all "clowns."

Mr. Hu Shih lectured at the Dongya Tongwen Academy in the 16th year of the Republic of China on the four thinkers of China in the past 300 years, Gu Yanwu, Yan Yuan, and Dai Zhen, besides Mr. Someone. I couldn't understand it after thinking hard. Now I understand, the ideal character in Hu Shih's mind is also the ideal character in Liu Tieyun's mind. Having found such a person, why not be happy? Moreover, Mr. Hu himself has already imitated him very closely, so he can go on stage without dressing up!

In this way, we can also understand why Mr. Hu Shih especially praised "The Travels of Lao Can" during the May Fourth Movement.

Summer Night 225

— Tianma

In the evening, the remaining heat of the day has not yet dissipated, and the wind is stagnant, not moving. Sitting indoors, I am sweating profusely. It feels like there are hundreds of hot worms crawling inside the blood vessels all over my body. I frantically wave the palm-leaf fan back and forth, and bean-sized beads of sweat are still streaming down my body. At this time, I thought of the loveliness of winter again, although in winter I had also cursed the severe cold that made people clumsy, timid, and decadent.

I remembered the words my father told me when I was a child, "A calm mind naturally cools down," so I turned on the electric light, moved the chair to the writing desk near the window, and randomly took a recently published book by Ms. Ding Ling, "Mother," from the bookshelf, intending to use forced reading to calm my chaotic thoughts. This method was indeed effective. In less than a quarter of an hour, the beads of sweat all over my body were dried by the gentle breeze blowing in from the window, and the palm-leaf fan naturally fell from my hand to my feet. I intimately felt the comfort after the heat.

However, another kind of annoyance followed, which was a small green worm with a sharp beak.

Probably because they were chasing the light, as soon as the electric light was turned on, these annoying little bugs flew in from outside the window in droves. At first, it was one or two: : : flying onto the lampshade, onto the desk, onto the pages of the book in my hand, onto my face, onto my hands. They made no sound, just crawling everywhere, or using their sharp beaks to peck at my face and hands with all their might, making people feel an extra uncomfortable slight itch and a surprise similar to being attacked by an unexpected enemy.

At this time, I didn't care at all about these petty clowns. When they flew onto the pages of the book, I just brushed them away with my hand; when they crawled on my face or hands, making me feel uncomfortable, I slapped them away with my hand. Immediately, a tiny corpse rolled to my feet. I only glanced at it with contempt, and still indifferently continued reading.

However, the green worms became more and more numerous. At this time, it was no longer one or two, but a large swarm: : : swarming and dancing in the air, making you dizzy. They flew onto the pages of the book, making the words look like pockmarks; they flew onto your face and hands, pecking here and there, making you at a loss; sometimes they would even fly into your clothes, and crawl gently like a thief, making you feel tingling all over, unable to catch them and unable to see them, so you had to put down the book and strip off your clothes to search. Moreover, this large group of clowns swarming and dancing actually made a lot of noise, squeaking, like the sound of silkworms eating mulberry leaves, which made people feel particularly uncomfortable.

This disturbance made me very angry. I threw down the book and stood up abruptly, using angry and cold eyes to scan this group of swarming and dancing pests. With a heart full of revenge and a desire to eliminate them quickly, I quickly grabbed the fly swatter and swatted frantically: : : swatted: : : swatted, once, twice, three times: : : and then tiny corpses formed one pile, two piles, three piles. I stood before these piles of corpses, like a hero returning in triumph, or like a cruel and vicious tyrant.

It seemed that the massacre with the fly swatter was not enough to extinguish the anger in my heart, not enough to express my hatred for that group of clowns, so I thought of even more cruel tortures. I used the tip of the pen as an instrument of torture, stabbing them one by one. I watched those pitifully small lives struggle in vain, and I lit a lighter one by one to burn them, until the corpses in a row emitted a foul odor. At this time, I was using the greatest determination to deal with this group of disturbers. I thought that such a crazy massacre and such terrible torture would surely exterminate this group of disturbers and restore me to the comfort of quietly reading.

However, my plan ultimately failed. Those hateful green worms seemed to know nothing of the terror of massacre. As long as there was light, they still came in droves, still swarming and dancing, still crawling everywhere, still pecking at my face and hands. I frantically wielded the fly swatter, and small corpses piled up layer upon layer, but those that died died, and those that came still came. In the end, I had exhausted all my strength, beads of sweat were streaming down, I was panting, and looking at these disturbers who were not afraid of death, I could only grind my teeth and be angry. I had no ability to resist, so I shouted loudly to my wife, "Let's go for a walk on the road." To be honest, I ran away. I had already failed in the hands of this group of disturbers.

For the first time, I understood the meaning of the word "group." I understood the greatness of the power of the masses.

Carrot Top 226

— IalesRenard, translated by Lin Qu

(End of the last words)

Le Pichon: What skill? Do you want me to send you to a shoemaker to be an apprentice, as if punching a nail? Carrot Top: A shoemaker's or anywhere else. I can earn my own food, I can gain freedom.

Le Pichon: Too late, my poor Carrot Top. I spent so much money to educate you, just for you to nail soles?

Carrot Top: But if I told you, Dad, that I once wanted to commit suicide, what would you do?

Le Pichon: You say it like it's a big deal, Carrot Top.

Carrot Top: I swear to you, just yesterday I still wanted to hang myself.

Le Pichon: And you are still alive. It can be seen that you didn't want to die. But thinking of your failed suicide, you proudly raise your head. You think death has only tempted you. Carrot Top, selfishness will make you sharp-tongued. You only care about yourself. You think you live alone in the world.

Carrot Top: Dad, my brother is happy, my sister is happy, if Mom doesn't deliberately mess with me, as you say, I can cut off my tongue to feed the cat. Finally, as for you, you are the head of the family, people are afraid of you, even Mom is afraid of you. She will never hinder your happiness. This proves that some people in humanity are happy.

Le Pichon: You stubborn little thing, talking nonsense. Can you see the secrets in everyone's heart? Do you already understand everything?

Carrot Top: About my own affairs, I understand, Dad; at least I am trying to make myself understand.

Le Pichon: Then, Carrot Top, don't think about getting happiness. I can predict that you will never be happier than you are now, never, never.

Carrot Top: That's possible.

Le Pichon: I advise you to be patient, protect yourself, and when you are an adult and can be independent, you will be free, you can disown us, change a family, or change your temperament and temper. Before that, you can try to gain an advantage for yourself, suppress your feelings, observe others, even those who live with you; this will be very interesting; I can guarantee you will get many unexpected comforts.

Carrot Top: Undoubtedly, other people also have their suffering. But I will only pity them tomorrow. Today, I want to demand justice for myself. Whose fate is not better than mine? I have a mother. This mother neither likes me, nor do I like her.

"And me, do you think I like her?" Le Pichon suddenly said, very anxiously.

After hearing these words, Carrot Top raised his eyes to his father. He looked at his calm face for a long, long time, his thick mustache, where a mouth that seemed too shy to speak was hiding, his wrinkled forehead, the three wrinkles on the corner of each eye, and the drooping eyelids that made him seem to be sleeping when he walked.

For a while, Carrot Top couldn't say a word. He was afraid that the joy hidden in his heart, and the hand that he had caught and almost forcibly held, would all fly away.

Then he clenched his fist, threatened the village that was dozing over there, in the darkness, and exclaimed exaggeratedly, "Evil woman! You are perfectly wicked. I hate you."

"Don't scream," Le Pichon said, "In any case, she is always your mother."

"Ah!" Carrot Top replied, and he appeared frank and cautious again. "I'm not saying that just because she's my mother."

Talks

Who Should Be Severely Reprimanded? 249

— Xiaozhi

Last week, the Shanghai Electric Power Company discovered that some users, colluding with mechanics, were engaging in shockingly large-scale electricity theft. After a thorough investigation by the police, several key criminals were arrested. It is said that a remaining suspect, Mr. Zhou (who studied in Japan to become an engineer), can imitate the lead seals on the screws of the electric meters with perfect accuracy (note: the seals were put in place by the Electric Power Company specifically to prevent electricity theft). He can also disassemble electric meters with high skill, adjust the dials to reduce the recorded electricity consumption, and then replace the meters with counterfeit lead seals. ::: He then contacts officials in the Electric Power Company who are responsible for this task on behalf of various factories, and later the factories provide him with a small reward. ::: The number of factories engaged in fraudulent activities is countless, and there is enough evidence to sue over twenty factories (note: nineteen of them are silk mills and silk weaving factories).

In the current social organization, of course, there are some so-called "gentlemen" and "upper-class Chinese" who will put on a facade of false rationality and say, "Shameless, lawless scum! Is theft acceptable or permitted by law? ::: A dignified returned student, what can't he do, that he has to do such a disgraceful thing! How lamentable! :::"

Indeed, indeed! The golden words of "decent", "content", and "law-abiding" "upper-class" gentlemen are the most beautiful and pleasing to the ear. However, on the other hand, we must truly calm our minds, use true reason, and at least pay attention to the following facts.

(1) How many students go abroad to study and return to China each year! Regardless of their actual knowledge, given the already overcrowded existing distribution system and the nepotistic nature of all sectors in China, is there still room to accommodate them? Of course, this refers to the group of poor students without connections. However, they are also human beings and have the same basic needs for life - they need to eat, they need to live and dress... But they cannot get any of these things, and they cannot just sit idly by and wait to starve to death. Naturally, the only way for the weaker ones who have a flawed or incomplete view of the current society and its system and who lack understanding and principles is to use their petty intelligence to engage in theft and other disgraceful acts that are "illegal" to the so-called "upper-class Chinese"! Knowing this, who should we severely reprimand? (2) According to reports, most of the factories engaged in fraudulent activities this time are silk mills and silk weaving factories. This shows the economic downturn in China's silk industry. China's silk production was once among the best in the world, but in recent years it has plummeted! On the one hand, this is indeed due to natural disasters, man-made calamities, and the failure of silk weavers to use scientific methods to improve production. On the other hand, it is truly due to the constraints of unequal treaties, which have allowed foreign artificial silk to dominate our entire silk market! (China's raw silk production is about 252,000 dan per year, while the amount of foreign artificial silk imported is also 130,891 dan!) Because of this, small-capitalized and poorly equipped Chinese silk mills are inevitably approaching collapse and decline. In the simple calculations of businessmen, "stealing electricity" is a small gain. As for "being dragged into the legal court," how could they not know about it?

In short: Theft is real, breaking the law is real, and being disgraceful to upper-class Chinese is also real, but their misguided views and lack of principles are even more real! In addition to these "realities," we must also recognize that social problems have become extremely acute. Of course, this is also a reality!

Sin 250

— Xian

One day, A Shun's father woke up. His wrinkled face was always so gloomy. Ever since he had owed more than thirty yuan last year, the villagers of 溪村 had never seen A Shun's father smile, except for the slight twitching of the corners of his mouth with a "Hmm, hmm." On this day, unexpectedly, after he got up, while washing his face with cold water, two "coo, coo" sounds entered A Shun's father's ears from the eaves. He dropped the washcloth in disbelief, stepped over the threshold, walked to the threshing ground, looked up, and two pigeons fluttered their wings and flew backward with "coo, coo" sounds. At this moment, A Shun's father smiled. It was a pity that his son and daughter-in-law did not see it. He muttered to himself again, "Hmm, hmm, it's going to rain one of these days."

As if he were pleased, he ran into the kitchen, swallowed two bowls of cold rice, wiped his mouth, picked up his ever-present dry tobacco pipe from the corner of the wall, and although he had not been to town for a long time to buy a bundle of dry tobacco for twelve copper coins, sucking on the empty pipe had the same effect. He walked to the threshing ground again like a leisurely farmer. The innocent singing of the duck herding girl, Zhao Jie, came from the riverbank. Today, A Shun's father was not annoyed by this song. He thought that Zhao Jie was a very likable child. The distant mountains were not yet illuminated by the sun at this time, and the sky was gloomy. "Coo, coo," this lovely bird of happiness flew over A Shun's father's head again. "Hmm, hmm, it's going to rain one of these days!" A Shun's father smiled, smiling like a child seeing someone selling candy.

A gust of wind blew, and A Shun's father seemed to feel a few raindrops on his face. He still didn't believe it, and when he stretched out his rough, dark palm, the rain became heavier and heavier. Suddenly, the sound of "It's raining!" cheered throughout the village. His son and daughter-in-law had already rushed from the shed. They were running so fast, and Zhao Jie, the duck herding girl, followed closely behind. A flock of ducks were racing along the bank of the field, "quack, quack."

"Dad, it's raining!" the son shouted, panting. Rain was falling on everyone's head, and everyone knew it was raining, but A Shun's father seemed to have just discovered it. He raised his head and looked at the sky. He absentmindedly wanted to smoke his dry tobacco pipe, took a few puffs, raised his dry tobacco pipe, and gently tapped it a few times on the rain-soaked threshing ground, as if to remove the ashes. A Shun watched his father's absentmindedness, and in his heart, he was calculating that since it was raining, this year's harvest would not be worse than last year's. As long as the price of rice rose when it was put on the market, after paying off the debt of more than thirty yuan, there would still be several tens of white silver pieces left over. Tomorrow, he would brave the rain to go to town to buy a bundle of dry tobacco for his father... In fact, as long as it rained, A Shun's father would no longer care about dry tobacco. He looked up at the sky, and the thought that turned in his mind was - the debt of more than thirty yuan.

He smiled slightly. "It's going to rain one of these days," he suddenly realized that the three of them were standing in the heavy rain as if they were frozen. "Grandpa A Shun, aren't you going inside to change your clothes?" After saying that, the three of them laughed.

That night, the old man did not mention the debt of more than thirty yuan, and the son did not feel the blisters on his feet throbbing. Laughter filled this small three-room cottage. A Shun had already obediently climbed into bed to sleep.

"As it was said, we country people never do bad things, sin - does heaven punish us by starving us to death?" Today, A Shun's father suffered from a laughing illness, and he laughed again without knowing it.

Secrets 251

— Ben

"Why has older sister become so beautiful?" This was a big question from the ten-year-old younger brother.

"Why isn't older sister like she used to be—always jumping, laughing, and immersed in innocent happiness? And mother is also acting strangely. In public, she wears a forced smile, but behind people's backs, she just sobs and sighs, especially late at night, or in the clear mornings at dawn." These were all things the young brother couldn't understand; he just pondered them secretly.

Because his older sister had become beautiful, the younger brother also began to have hopeful dreams, which truly troubled the gray-haired, frail mother. The younger brother often threw up his old, tattered clothes and threw himself into his mother's arms, scratching his little mouth and saying: "Mommy, older sister is wearing pretty clothes, I want to wear them too!" This was like a sharp knife cutting at the mother's heart, but she could only suppress the grief rising in her throat and say in an unnatural, loving tone:

"Good boy, don't pester me. When you grow up like your older sister, I'll make you two sets too. It's not popular now—and, good boy, you need to understand things. Even if I made them for you now, wouldn't you just ruin them when you go scavenging in the trash?"

"Um, um, I want them::: When I go scavenging, I know to take them off and leave them at home!"

"Good boy, stop pestering me. Hurry up and shoulder your bamboo basket to find a living. Go early, come back early, and don't loiter outside. Come here, I've saved a bowl of cold noodles for you to eat. Alas!"

When the younger brother heard his mother's "Alas," he immediately glanced at her face. At that moment, his mother's face truly startled him—pale and cloudy, a mask full of wrinkles. He automatically left her embrace. Having cold noodles to eat was, of course, another reason he stopped pestering her.

Two years ago, their hometown suffered a devastating flood. In the middle of a stormy night with thunder and lightning, the father put on a raincoat and bamboo hat to try and reinforce the dam, but unfortunately, he never returned. The next morning, the whole family was floating in a watery world. Fortunately, a boat carrying refugees from a distant village passed by. After much pleading, the mother, older sister, and younger brother were rescued. They floated along, eventually drifting into this paradise-like city.

After arriving in the city, the mother and her two children experienced a period of begging door to door.

Later, the older sister found work in a silk factory, the younger brother shouldered his bamboo basket to scavenge through the trash cans along the streets, and the mother, with her gray hair, stayed home and ate whatever they could find. People saw that they were very poor, but in a dark, damp kitchen, the family of three was reunited and quite happy.

Unfortunately, less than three months later, the silk factory shut down, so the older sister also stayed home all day. Mother and daughter stared at each other, and the hardship of life was beyond words. Therefore, the younger brother's work became even more urgent, and he had to shoulder his bamboo basket late into the night to scavenge for a living in the streets and alleys.

One night, it was already late, and he was squatting next to a trash can on the street when suddenly a young man, holding a woman's hand, flew past him and went into a brightly lit hotel ahead.

Page 21

He saw clearly that the woman was indeed his older sister. He wanted to chase after them, but in an instant, they were gone. So, feeling gloomy, he shouldered his bamboo basket and went home. Because of this, he didn't even bother to pick up cigarette butts, rotten cloth, paper scraps, and other things he could sell along the way.

When he got home, he blurted out this question to his mother: "Mom, I just saw older sister holding a strange man's hand going into a big hotel. Who was that? What were they doing? Why didn't they take us with them? Mommy, I want two new sets of clothes too!"

"Bah, are you crazy? Your older sister clearly went back to work—stop pestering me! What new clothes? I told you a long time ago, when you're big, as big as your older sister, I'll definitely make them for you::: How much did you find today?"

"Um, um, um, only two hundred cash, and I ate six cash worth of cold noodles."

In the crowing of the rooster at dawn, the younger brother, full of questions, vaguely heard his older sister's voice, his mother opening the door, followed by "I was so sleepy!", "I've been waiting for you half the night!", "Two dollars!" Alas!" A few miserable sounds.

Correspondences from Store Clerks

Unbearable Responsibility 252

Editor:

I have a matter that I wanted to ask you about. However, I have been hesitant to do so because I am afraid that my lack of knowledge and poor writing skills may result in an inadequate expression. But now the reality is unbearable. Therefore, I would like to respectfully present the detailed events as follows:

My teacher—who runs a store in a rural town—also assumed the responsibility of collecting land taxes three years ago (that is, the local bailiff). At that time, all the local property owners (that is, landowners) were responsible for guaranteeing him to the county government. Unfortunately, in recent years, the rural economy has suddenly collapsed, and all the rural households are struggling to find food, let alone pay the annually increasing land taxes on desolate tombs and dilapidated houses. As a result, the amount owed by the bailiff has gradually increased. Until May of last year, the bailiff was detained and held for payment. However, after he was detained, no one raised funds, and there was no way to raise funds. According to the old practice of the county, if the bailiff is unable to manage, the original guarantor should be responsible for handling it. However, although the county government issued a warrant to summon the responsible property owners, after they made some efforts with the people in the county government, the county government no longer mentioned it. Now, more than a year has passed, and my teacher himself feels that prison life is unbearable, and his family is suffering extremely. Therefore, he is willing to declare bankruptcy to resolve the matter. However, he himself is in prison, his wife is a rural woman, and his children are young. They don't know what to do. Now, he and his family have entrusted the incompetent and powerless me to handle the matter. Therefore, I respectfully ask you, the wise one, to give me detailed instructions. I would be deeply grateful! (1) What procedures can be used to make the county government execute bankruptcy? (2) Can private debts owed at the time of bankruptcy be included? (3) Will there be further lawsuits after voluntary bankruptcy? (4) Although the total assets may not be enough to cover the debts, is there any reason to request a certain amount for the family's living expenses? (5) If a lawyer is hired to handle the matter, can the litigation and legal fees be paid from the assets?

Wishing you good health! Respectfully, Store Clerk Zhang Hua

Editor's Note: This case cannot be resolved by bankruptcy alone. If your teacher has indeed embezzled tax money, then in addition to seizing his property, he must also be detained and pursued for the full amount. After the full amount has been recovered, he will also be punished. The source of tax revenue, which is vital to the country, cannot be arbitrarily embezzled by the tax collectors. If your teacher has not embezzled anything, and the tax shortfall is indeed due to the people's failure to pay, then your teacher has no responsibility at all. The county government's abuse of authority in detaining an innocent person for years is an inappropriate punishment that can be appealed to the provincial government and the Department of Finance in accordance with the Administrative Appeal Law. Once you apply for bankruptcy compensation, the embezzlement charge will be confirmed.

When each county collects land taxes, it must create a printed receipt book. The first copy is for notification, the second copy is a receipt, called a license, and the third copy is a . In theory, before the is opened, the should be handed over to the tax collectors for distribution. The property owners, based on the amount on the , seal and deliver the payment, and obtain the license as proof. For any property owner who has not completed the payment, the license should be connected to the stub. After the deadline, the collection office should open and engrave a clear list, and hand it over to the tax collectors for supervision. Therefore, "self-sealed delivery to the counter" and "receipt (license) not separated from the stub" are truly the heavenly principles of the tax system. However, the results of actual investigations show that very few counties can handle it this way. Most counties nominally make changes, but in reality, they reserve room for fraud. Now, let's write down two of the most common so-called changes in various counties: (1) Some counties create the printed receipts very late; for example, even in the 22nd year of the Republic of China (1933), they have not completed the creation of the receipts for the 20th year. What they rely on to collect taxes is a small ticket. Each field has a printed stub, which has a number and indicates the amount of silver to be paid. Unless the full amount is paid, it cannot be cut from the stub. A small ticket, however, is just a temporary receipt, it is not limited to one for each field, and the amount is filled in at any time. Therefore, in these counties, if I owe 1,000 yuan in taxes this year, I can negotiate with the collection office to pay half of it first. If you have enough face, you can even pay less. Therefore, there are often many people without power whose taxes are paid by the big gentry. Small households pay 70-80% of the tax to the big households, the big households pay 50-60% of the tax to the county government, and the county government only remits 40-50% to the provincial government. Layer upon layer of embezzlement, officials and gentry colluding in broad daylight. (2) In many counties, after the receipts are created, the first notification copy and the second license copy are cut off at the same time and handed over to the tax collectors for collection. This method also has many drawbacks. To put it bluntly, once the stub is separated, it can be considered as fully received; to put it mildly, it can also be considered as not received at all. According to the editor's investigation, almost every tax collector in these counties is cheating, but some are just more daring than others. We don't blame them too much, because this system really has a seductive effect. Zhang's teacher probably encountered this kind of county, so the editor does not fully believe that he is completely free of wrongdoing (or is he wrong?). Now that the county government has spoken officially, it is difficult to tell the truth. For now, we believe that he should try to hand over the embezzled money himself. For those who have truly not received the money, he can contact all the tax collectors and truthfully report the matter to the county government. They are bound to feel sympathy and help. Moreover, for the sake of a permanent solution, he should demand the implementation of the "self-sealed delivery to the counter, receipt not separated from the stub" method, so as to avoid suffering the loss of this "official talk" again.

The editor is from Jiading County, not far from Shanghai. There are certainly many politics that we can't stand in our area, but the collection system is indeed handled reasonably well. Self-sealed delivery to the counter and stub not separated from the receipt have been implemented for a long time. Our tax payment procedure is very similar to buying a train ticket at the train station. Even if we are short one or two coppers, the license cannot be cut off; we would rather have the money returned. The tax collectors' responsibility is only to urge; at worst, they will be dismissed. The provincial government's Department of Finance can only urge other counties to remit the money; it cannot urge us in Jiading, because in the end, the county government can submit a request to check the stubs, as ironclad proof of whether there is money or not. However, this method is also very beneficial to tax revenue: in normal years, the amount collected within twelve months is always between 90% and 95%. Other counties probably do not have such a good record. It can be seen that the method of making changes is completely a method of cheating.

Novel

Under the Traffic Lights (12) 253

— Xilin

"The master won't be coming tonight, why so many dishes?"

"There's also Mr. Li..." Long Hair's words were always short and to the point.

"Mr. Li?" Auntie A-zhen, this young woman, had become very alert after being trained by the concubine. She quickly pretended to have misspoke and said, "Oh, that's right!"

Coincidentally, Mr. Li came downstairs to find a match to light a cigarette. A-zhen deliberately flattered him and said,

"Mr. Li, dinner is almost ready, don't go out?" A knowing smile spread across her face, her eyes rolling upward as she watched Shi Qiao's face. Truly, A-zhen's smile, pure and innocent, was sometimes more charming than the third concubine. Shi Qiao didn't answer her. He lit his cigarette and went back upstairs.

The third concubine wouldn't let time go to waste. She overheard the sound of leather shoes going upstairs and peeked out from the door.

"Li, Li:::" She felt the difficulty of addressing him for the first time. If she called him Mr. Li, it would sound like she was addressing her own cousin, and people would be suspicious, wouldn't they? Calling him by his name alone didn't sound like she was addressing an elder! Calling him "brother" was also awkward! And, no matter how bold a woman you were, it would be a bit embarrassing! Fortunately, her expressive eyes had already made Shi Qiao walk towards her.

"You just got back? Come, come sit here!" She pulled Shi Qiao to a long sofa and sat down next to him. Shi Qiao absentmindedly looked at her legs—she deliberately

"Don't, don't, you bad thing!"

Shi Qiao smiled slightly, tossed his messy hair back, and stared at her face, which was smugly looking at him askance. The third concubine believed that this angle of looking askance showed Shi Qiao's best features: his hair was still messy, his nose was high, his lips were thin, and his jaw forcefully outlined a long face. Looking down, his often-washed clothes had shrunk, tightly showing off the muscles of his whole body. His arms, bent forward, showed a kind of masculine brute force::::: The third concubine's imagination came more quickly than a man seeing a woman's flesh. She was used to seeing men in society who were polished and refined, those were all bland apples. Ah, look, this is such a stimulating coconut, a tropical coconut!

But the coconut was still thinking about some things—like what happened to Zhang Honglie and Zhou Shaoping today, whether the Student Volunteer Army was organized, and the matter of planning a magazine to promote resistance against Japan. These things were, of course, things that the third concubine did not understand and did not want to understand. But Shi Qiao had never thoroughly understood them either! Moreover, these things were not going smoothly, and he was feeling upset and unhappy.

Soon, wine came to relieve his boredom. The table was piled high with dishes, and he ate shamelessly.

Film Special

Small Company's Production Sees the Light of Day Again 254

— Xing

= The Central Film Censorship Committee Opens the Door to Convenience: The Release of Films with Supernatural, Sensual, and Martial Arts Themes

Since 1931, after the Central Film Censorship Committee adopted a strict approach, countless domestically produced Chinese films have been banned. As a result, the atmosphere in the film industry became clear, and the spirit of the film industry was boosted. However, the number of films released sharply declined, and many companies went out of business. In two years, small companies have been eliminated, and now there are less than thirty left.

Crude and poorly made films are not often seen now. However, in the past year, more than a hundred films produced by small companies have not been approved by the Central Committee. So, in the spring of 1933, eighteen small companies jointly submitted a petition to the Central Committee, and surprisingly, they achieved considerable results not long ago.

It is said that in order to sympathize with business difficulties and maintain the future of domestically produced films, the Central Committee formulated a special method and issued a "Temporary Permit for the Public Screening of Unapproved Domestically Produced Films." The deadline is six months. All domestically produced films, whether screened or not, that have been banned can receive this preferential treatment. As a result, the banned films surprisingly had the good fortune to see the light of day again.

Although the period is only six months (from June 15 to December 15 of this year), each film can be shown unhindered throughout the country during those six months. Even if it cannot make money, it can at least recover part of the capital invested in filming. Small companies can maintain their business for a few more years with this unexpected income. Or, in these two or three years, they may be able to shoot a few more good films, which would be of great benefit to the future of domestically produced films. This must be said to be a virtuous policy of the gentlemen of the Central Film Censorship Committee. But:::

This not only benefits small companies, but also benefits small cinemas in the interior. In order to cater to the tastes of local residents, most inland cinemas specialize in screening domestically produced films. In the past two years, only a few large companies have produced them. The quantity is small, and the rental price is high. Demand exceeds supply, and there is a constant sense of film shortage. In the past six months, due to the impact of economic depression, there has been a situation of bankruptcy. This time, the products of small companies are coming in an endless stream, which is no different from a cloudburst in a severe drought, and indirectly they have also received the blessing of the Central Committee. It kills several birds with one stone (and some residents in the interior can also feast their eyes and satisfy their low-level interests). Of course, it is also a good move.

As far as I know, small companies have shipped more than forty films to the interior in the past ten days. It is estimated that at least ten films will be screened in Shanghai in July. Two-thirds of them are represented by the Lianhua Company or the Central Company. Of course, films with sensual and martial arts flavors occupy a significant place, and the number of films with supernatural themes is also alarming. Perhaps the Mingxing Company's "Burning of the Red Lotus Temple" and the Youlian Company's "Female Knight Errant of the Desolate River" will become popular again and reappear in Shanghai.

Of course, everything has its advantages and disadvantages. Once this trend starts, what impact will it have on morality and people in various parts of the country, especially in the interior where culture is closed and superstition is deeply rooted? We have not yet had time to discuss in depth whether the original principles that the Central Film Censorship Committee used to ban films have been abandoned. But we can see that the surface purpose of the Central Film Censorship Committee is to maintain the small companies that produce domestically made films. In today's situation of empty national treasury and social depression, perhaps this is also a "stopgap measure" in a situation where there is no other way (as said by a certain member of the Central Committee). However, I hope that a fundamental solution will appear in the near future.

Audience Opinions

After Watching "The Road to Fitness" 255

— Xu Hairong

The theme of this film is really novel. It uses the life of street performers who wander the world as a background to write about the cruelty of the old society. We can vaguely see a hideous face of the old society on the screen.

Speaking of the entire script, we acknowledge that its consciousness is good, but there are some flaws. For example, Yun Sheng, a wealthy man's son, is also eager to talk about love when his studies have not been successful and he cannot live independently. And in order to achieve his ultimate goal, he actually breaks his engagement with his original fiancée and marries his lover, the street performer. Although his kind of classless love is pure, when we criticize him from an objective point of view, this kind of behavior of rushing to talk about marriage and disregarding his own studies is not a proper path for a young person to take.

The director's skill is very good. He has staged a very complex and tortuous story in an orderly manner, so that the audience does not feel any boredom from beginning to end. This is where he succeeded. However, I think that his depiction of the death of Ye Feifei's grandmother and mother is a bit too long, so that the script cannot be very compact, which is a pity.

Close-up of Luo Kebang, the protagonist of Lianhua Second Factory's "Little Toys," taken by Ke Ming and presented by Wu Zesheng

After Watching "A Modern Woman" 256

— Yu Hong

This is a work written and starring by Ai Xia herself. Although it cannot be said to be an experience talk based on her own experiences, it is at least better than those who create stories behind closed doors, right? But although the expression is so realistic, there are still many contradictory points in the consciousness.

Isn't there a slogan here that shouts "Thorough love"? But can the love process and motivation between Jiang Tao Tao and Yu Leng be said to be "thorough"? Tao Tao is a romantic woman. She doesn't know what chastity is, she only knows how to seek satisfaction of sexual desire; Yu Leng is a restrained man, he doesn't know what love is, he only needs money and life. Their so-called "thorough love" is based on sexual desire and money. So even if Tao Tao doesn't commit a crime and Yu Leng doesn't back out, their ending will not be good, because love is not like this at all.

On "A Modern Woman" 257

— Mei Cun

The objects of the concept of love for modern women in today's society are mostly nothing more than money and handsome men. Some only need money and are satisfied with material comfort. Some want to find men who are both wealthy and handsome and of comparable age. When any one of them is dissatisfied, they will boldly disregard the law, morality, reputation, etc., and commit various crimes and dark secrets.

Jiang Tao Tao, the protagonist in "A Modern Woman," belongs to the latter type. The original theme of such a good background could have revealed the dark secrets as much as possible, if the script itself did not stick to anyone's past facts. However, the various tragedies and comedies produced by the diverse prosperity of society cannot be fully depicted in "A Modern Woman."

Wasn't that reporter an old friend of Tao Tao? After not seeing each other for three years, there must be a more intimate feeling after a long separation, but a few days after they met, Tao Tao asked him, "Do you love me?" The reporter was stunned, and it didn't seem like he was hesitant. It was really embarrassing. The death of his child, the loss of his job, his loving wife's divorce, and his mistress's imprisonment must have been the most tragic and heart-wrenching time for Yu Leng, but the screen did not give the audience any deep or tense feeling. Tao Tao met her friend An Lin after she was imprisoned. They should have been surprised at each other, but it wasn't explained. Aren't these minor flaws?

After Seeing "Spring Water Love Waves" 258

— Heshan

Every day when I open the newspaper, I am struck by news of abduction, rape, fraud, abandonment, and so on. The cruel unfolding of a deformed society has cultivated countless dark sins. "Food and sex" are inherent human nature, especially for the wealthy class who are "well-fed and warm," they treat women as excellent forms of entertainment. At the same time, women's vain pursuits and weak will have become a common phenomenon in today's society. Especially today, after the semi-abandonment of the restraints of traditional ethics, and without the true realization of women's liberation, it gives men an easy opportunity to attack.

"Spring Water Love Waves" is a film that exposes this kind of sin. It loudly calls to awaken the illusions of women who are being played with, and especially gives a strong warning to those who abuse women. The consciousness is quite healthy. At least it is more relevant to the needs than unrealistic and empty questions.

What cannot be buried in this film is the director's contribution. He used light and skillful techniques, cleverly connecting the extremely ordinary story, narrating it in such a compact and profound way. The pictures are not wasted at all, and the descriptions are very powerful. Regarding the sorrow of A Mao's encounter, it especially grasps the sympathy of everyone. Every change and evolution in the play, and the contrast between bitterness and joy, all seem natural and reasonable. In terms of performance, no major shortcomings can be found.

The Slump of Hollywood Directors 259

— Shichun

The slump in Hollywood is now being created piece by piece. The actors have already felt the panic of the environment, and the directors may not be affected by this trend, but the devastated Hollywood cannot maintain the dignity of the directors after all.

Now there are four directors in Hollywood who are panicking because they have been idle for a long time without getting work. They have no way to maintain their lives, so they united and came up with a wonderful method. They gave up directing work and became actors. What a sad thing this is! One of these four directors is the famous Karl Vores, who has been a director in Hollywood for more than ten years. Fifteen years ago, a Broncho Billy he directed received unparalleled reputation, but now he can't even maintain his life. What a pity. There is also Ferre P. Smalley, who once enjoyed the reputation of first-class director in Universal, is now also idle in Hollywood, unable to find work to solve the bread problem. There is also a beast film director Frank P., and the most embarrassed one is called Sa Mairs Li Gai, who is heavily in debt, owing thousands of dollars. Because the directing life could not support their own bodies, these four directors lowered their status and acted in a film, acting as actors themselves. The film is called "Power and Glory," and of course it is a work full of depictions of bitterness.

New Film Introduction 260

"Trouble in the Abdomen"

Also known as "Suppressing Communists in Southern Jiangxi"

The Communist bandits in Jiangxi, Guangdong, Fujian, Hunan, and Hubei are indeed the "trouble in the abdomen" of our nation. Last autumn, under the pressure of the central army, they invaded south in droves, hoping to occupy Guangdong as a base. Fortunately, Chen Jitang, the commander-in-chief of the Southern Route Communist Suppression, was prepared and led his troops to cooperate in the suppression, driving the Communist bandits back to their old nest. The fierceness of the battle and the greatness of the sacrifice are the most worthy of record in the history of communist suppression.

"Trouble in the Abdomen" is a battle film taken on the battlefield at the risk of death by the accompanying journalist at the time. The content ranges from the communist bandits' invasion of the south to the overcoming of the bandit areas, with very detailed records. The brightness of the light in this film is the best of all war films. It has now been shipped to Shanghai and is scheduled to be premiered at the Capital Grand Theater in Nanjing on the 28th. As for Shanghai, it has been decided to be premiered at the Beijing Grand Theater.

The Song of Songs Movie Novel The Song of Songs (4) 261

— Siping

After Wahlduk finished carving, he happily said whether this time it looked like it. Next time, he would carve a marble statue. A knock on the door startled them, and Lily quickly hid behind the curtain to put on her clothes.

The uninvited guest was a tall soldier, wearing a military officer's uniform, with gray hair, a stiff mustache on his mouth, and wearing a pair of glasses. One look at him knew he was a pervert. The alluring eyes saw Lily fleeing behind the curtain and jumped out of fire. The officer was Count Mazi Bashiber, and Wahlduk did not dare to offend him, so he reluctantly shook hands with him. The Count said that he was passing by here, saw the lights in the room, so he came in to ask if the stone statue carved for him was ready.

Lily dressed and shyly walked out from behind the curtain. The officer stared at her at a glance, said "Good!" and turned to ask Wahlduk to introduce him. Wahlduk reluctantly did the introduction. Lily gave a village girl's salute, but the Count solemnly lowered his head and kissed her jade hand. He treated her like a noble lady. He used his seductive means to get her to talk. But Lily was a little scared in front of this stranger, fearing that her aunt would wake up at this time. She sat uncomfortably and was about to leave. When Wahlduk sent her out the door, he whispered to ask her if she would come again tomorrow night. Lily also whispered back to see.

When Wahlduk came back, the Count looked at him with malicious intent, knowing that Lily was just Wahlduk's model. The Count privately thought he had a plan.

He turned his deceptive tricks and thought of going to the bookstore. That old monster is easy to deal with. He can find out her price soon. As for the young sculptor's resistance, there is no need to worry about it. In the Count's eyes, the girl herself is also not a concern. He is an old hand at playing with women with money::::: (To be continued)
